Record of the Fifth Day of the Noulens Case Trial

▲Noulens and Wang Refuse to Sign the Trial Records

▲The Court Appoints a Lawyer to Defend Noulens and Wang

The Jiangsu Higher Court continued to hear the Noulens and Wang Delizeng case of endangering the Republic of China at the Jiangning Local Court at 9 AM on the 16th. The judges present were as before, and lawyer Chen Ying also attended. After the judges ascended the bench, the presiding judge, Li Mian, first said to the defendant's lawyer, Chen Ying, "This case has been heard several times, and your lawyer has never spoken in defense. Now the interrogation is about to end. Your lawyer, for the sake of protecting the legal interests of the defendant, if you think there is anything that needs to be defended, you can give full play to it, but please do not speak outside the scope of defense." Chen Ying said that the defendant had objections to the competent authorities in this case and only entrusted our lawyer to attend the court to record the proceedings and did not authorize our lawyer to defend, so it was not convenient to speak. The clerk was then ordered to read out the records of the three trials on the 10th, 11th, and 12th of this month, which were translated by the translator Yang Zhaolong. At the beginning of the reading, Noulens repeatedly raised various issues outside the scope of the recorded confession, or because he was not familiar with the order of the recorded confession, he argued loudly, bringing up irrelevant matters. The judge said that the purpose of reading this record was to prevent errors in the record that would hinder the defendant's interests. If the defendant thought there was an error, he could only declare it at any time and request correction, but could not raise supplementary words that would not be consistent with the original confession. If he debated like this at every point, it was feared that even the entire time of this court would not be enough to read the record. Later, Noulens requested that a copy of the record be given to him for verification, and the court agreed. The reading was then continued. Whenever there were important key points, such as the identification of evidence and the relationship with the Communist Party, the defendant and the lawyer scrutinized and translated each word and sentence, which took a lot of time. Whenever the defendant thought that there was indeed an error and made a reasonable request for correction, it was corrected at any time. It was not until 12:30 that the reading was completed.

The presiding judge then called Noulens and Wang Delizeng to sign, but Noulens and Wang said that they did not understand the Chinese records and did not know the corrected content, so they refused to sign. The presiding judge then presented Noulens with the English list of items seized from the Nanjing Road and other houses. Noulens then raised arguments against the items on the English list, bit by bit, extremely complicated and trivial. At 1:20 PM, the presiding judge announced that the court would be adjourned for today and could be questioned again tomorrow. Noulens was still talking endlessly. The presiding judge asked lawyer Chen Ying, "Now there is something I want to ask, that is, can your lawyer be responsible to this court for defending the parties?" Chen stated that the parties only authorized the recording and correction of translation rights, and as for the right to defend, he had declared in court earlier that it was canceled. The presiding judge said that since Chen was absent , sitting in the lawyer's seat in the courtroom, problems have arisen. Noulens also made a statement on , and the two sides argued for a long time. The presiding judge said that since the party had no lawyer, according to the Criminal Procedure Law, the presiding judge could appoint two lawyers to defend the party. He appointed two people, one of whom was good at German and English, and asked Noulens whether he recognized them. Noulens said that since it had not been agreed to by him, it would be difficult to admit it. Again, there was a long argument. The presiding judge then announced that he would be interrogated again tomorrow (the 17th) at 8 AM and adjourned the court. It was already 1:55 PM.

Severe Drought in Jiangxi Province

▲Tiger Plague Spreads Everywhere, Many Deaths

A dispatch from Nanchang states that at the beginning of summer in this province, there were continuous heavy rains and floods. The fields along the Gan River, Fu River, and Poyang Lake were completely submerged, and many of the dikes built with work-for-relief programs also collapsed and have not been repaired to this day. After the floods, it has not rained since June 20th, nearly two months, and the hot sun has been shining, with no rain at all, which has had a profound impact on agriculture. At the time of the busy harvest last month, farmers not only had to use waterwheels to irrigate the late rice, but also had to draw water to plant the second-season rice. The wage for short-term labor increased from three cents to one yuan, but there were still no workers to hire. Very few of the soybeans for the second-season rice were planted. Currently, the fields in higher areas are already withered and cracked, and the fields in lower areas are also dry because the lakes, ports, ponds, and springs have all been dried up, and the green rice has also turned withered. The land is scorched for thousands of miles, and it is feared that there will be no harvest at all. In recent days, although there have been occasional dark clouds and faint thunder, it is still just the sky being dry and the rain not falling, just a sigh of relief for the poor. In Linchuan, Xinjian, Nanfeng, and other places, not only the fields are withered, but the drinking water in the wells has also caused panic. The Xinjian County government has received countless disaster reports from various districts, all of which state that it has not rained for a long time, the rice seedlings have all withered, the land is scorched for thousands of miles, there will be no harvest, and they request that the provincial government be petitioned to reduce the land tax and provide relief to the disaster victims. The county magistrate has reported the situation to the Department of Civil Affairs of the provincial government.

Currently, the tiger plague is raging, which is due to the lack of rain, increased heat, dry air, and flying dust, which are enough to increase the power of the tiger plague. Therefore, the tiger plague has spread almost all over the province. In the past month, the number of people who have died of the plague in Nanchang, Raozhou, Jingzhen, Leping, Zhangshu, Gao'an, and other places has been in the thousands. Recently, the plague in Linchuan, Yugan, Fuliang, and other places has continued to increase, and has spread from cities to villages. According to a visitor from Linchuan, more than a thousand people have died in the county seat in the past month, and members of the county party department and the chief of the local court have all contracted the tiger plague, vomiting and diarrhea, and dying within a few hours. Poor people often have entire families perish. The supply of coffins cannot meet the demand, which has not been seen in decades. A group of ignorant people do not know how to properly prevent the epidemic and only know how to pray to gods and worship Buddha. Within a month, the cost of holding religious ceremonies in Linchuan was more than 50,000 yuan, and the cost of rural superstitions is not included. According to medical circles, with this amount of money used for proper epidemic prevention, the entire county can be universally injected with serum and vaccines, which is truly incomprehensible. According to a letter from Ji'an, after the tiger plague broke out in the county, people could be seen dying one after another. According to a survey, more than 70 people died in three days. A letter from Ganzhou states that the tiger plague has spread from Nanxiong to Ganzhou, and patients can die within a few hours. The city was captured by bandits last year and then besieged by bandits, and all medicines have long been exhausted, and there is nothing that can be done to provide relief. In Nanchang city, after the well water was disinfected and the citizens were universally vaccinated, the epidemic has slowed down slightly, but the spread from the city to the countryside has intensified. In the Wanshou Palace area of Xinjian, the tiger plague is rampant, and countless people have died. In the Chen family in Zhuyuan, more than 40 people died in ten days out of more than 50 households, which is truly shocking. (August 13th)

Urgent Reports from Various Dangerous Sections of the Lu and Yellow Rivers

▲ Water Level Rises to Last Year's Highest Point

▲ County Magistrates Along the River Ordered by Han to Reside on the Riverbank

Jinan Dispatch: Recently, due to continuous autumn rains, the water level of the Yellow River has been rising continuously in the upper, middle, and lower reaches. At Dongzhuang in the upper reaches, the water level has reached 58.37 meters, equaling the highest water level of last year. Other sections are also nearly at last year's peak. Chairman of Shandong Province, Han Fuqu, telegraphed River Affairs Bureau Director Zhang Lianjia this morning, as well as the county magistrates of the 21 counties along the riverbanks—Yuncheng, Pu, Fan, Shou Zhang, Yanggu, Dong'a, Pingyin, Feicheng, Changqing, Qihe, Licheng, Jiyang, Huimin, Bin County, Lijin, Heze, Dongping, Zhangqiu, Qidong, Qingcheng, and Putai—ordering them to immediately move to the riverbanks in person to devote their full energy to supervising the emergency repairs and strengthen the defenses. They are not permitted to return to their counties until the water level drops by two feet. River Affairs Bureau Director Zhang Lianjia also telegraphed all river workers to work day and night, personally supervising the emergency repairs. They must especially and thoroughly inspect the dikes and dams for weak spots, holes, and rat burrows. River Affairs Bureau personnel will also work as usual, regardless of day, night, or weekends, with the work being extraordinarily tense. At the Zhukou dangerous section on the border of Hebei and Shandong, the main current is eroding the bank, and the pressed hemp bags and bricks are almost level with the water. The main current at Lisheng Village is directly impacting the ninth and tenth dams with exceptional force. The ninth dam is visibly collapsing by the day, and the tenth dam has one break underwater. The beach opposite Wang Zaojia in the lower reaches has been scoured away by the current, and the current is gradually shifting downward, with extremely strong scouring force. The revetments downstream are under increasing pressure, and two sections of the revetments have shifted. Zhang Lianjia is currently still at that site, supervising the work day and night, braving the rain to lead the emergency repairs. Today, the water level at Luokou has risen by 1.8 centimeters, reaching a level of 29.87 meters. The telegram from Han Fuqu to the county magistrates is recorded below: "To River Affairs Bureau Director and all County Magistrates along the River: Given the continuous rise in the Yellow River and the approaching autumn winds, it is extremely easy for accidents to occur. The lives and property of countless people will be submerged. As county magistrates, you bear an inescapable responsibility for your localities. You must devote your full energy to focusing on defense and immediately move to the riverbanks in person to supervise the work. You may only return to your posts after the water level has dropped by two feet and I, the Chairman, have approved it by telegram. You must all strictly comply with this order and report back. Chairman Han, sealed on a cold day." (August 15th)

All Circles in Anhui Participate in the Anti-War Alliance

▲ Representatives Selected to Attend the General Assembly in Shanghai

Wuhu Dispatch: The Anhui Provincial Chamber of Commerce Federation and the Wuhu County Chamber of Commerce, along with all sectors of society, have joined the Anti-Civil War Alliance. As the alliance is scheduled to hold a general assembly on August 27th, Song Ziheng, the president of the Bank of China, has been specially recommended as a representative to attend in Shanghai. The proposal has also been sent to the assembly in advance. The original text is as follows: "Since the restoration of our country, those in power should have taken advantage of the national desire for governance and the opportunity presented by the European war to enlighten the people, develop industry, improve military preparedness, and strive for good governance. Even if we could not dominate East Asia, we would not have been humiliated by powerful neighbors. However, years of internal warfare have continued endlessly, causing useful young men and vast amounts of weapons to be sacrificed and consumed in the mutual struggle for territory without any value. Alas, first, we were suppressing remnants of warlords, then suppressing communists and bandits. The whole country was in a state of panic, with no peaceful years. Coupled with years of disasters and poor harvests, we are financially and physically exhausted, leading to the humiliation of Shenyang and the humiliation of Shanghai, one after another. The situation is as precarious as a pile of eggs. Now, to abolish internal warfare and avoid the irreversible disaster, we respectfully offer our views for adoption: (1) Refuse to allow the country to issue internal war bonds, mortgage loans, or advance collection of land taxes; refuse all financial supplies of gold and silver. (2) Refuse private requisitioning of ships, vehicles, horses, and labor by those engaged in internal warfare; refuse material support. (3) Persuade officers and soldiers of the army and navy not to serve private internal warfare. (4) Persuade railway and shipping workers not to serve private internal warfare." (August 14th)

Local Dispatches

Songjiang

▲ Case of Son Assaulting Mother in Xinzhuang Brought to Justice: A man surnamed Chen in Xinzhuang, who is quite wealthy, has three sons. His mother, Madam Chen Wang, is nearly sixty years old. The eldest son, Guangxin, is married and has his own family. The mother divided the household for her sons, and Guangxin lives alone in the old house, while the second son lives in the new house. Recently, because the second son is studying away from home, he rented out the residence. Unexpectedly, Guangxin, for some unknown reason, went to his brother's house, smashed the doors and windows. When the old mother came out to stop him, he brutally beat her, injuring her arm, which is now bruised. The matter was reported to the Public Security Sub-station, which arrested Guangxin. The victim, Chen Wang, also reported the situation. Local people believe that such an act of impiety and brutality against one's own parent should be punished. The patrol officer prepared a document and sent him to Songjiang on the 16th. After a preliminary hearing by the Public Security Bureau, he was ordered to be sent to the County Court for trial.

▲ Flourishing of the Insurance Business After the Fire: Since Dafeng Silk Shop in this city was careless, causing a fire that spread to several neighboring houses, resulting in considerable losses, insurance companies from Shanghai have sent representatives to Songjiang to establish branch offices and develop business. The Chinese-owned Anping Co., Ltd. has already been established, and Cai Guangzhao and Liu Fenghao have been appointed as agents for the Songjiang area. All nearby towns and cities are within their business scope. The office was established at Chengda Money Exchange and opened on the 16th. There was a large turnout from all sectors. It is said that the insurance department of the British-owned Jardine Matheson & Co. has also sent representatives to Songjiang to organize an office. The insurance business is springing up like mushrooms after rain, and merchants are happy to make contact to protect their property.

▲ Niu Yongjian Agrees to Serve as Director of the Plague Hospital: The Songjiang Red Cross Branch received a letter from Niu Yongjian yesterday, saying, "To Chairman Xue Wen: After reading your letter, I humbly accept the resolution of the fourth meeting of the Songjiang Branch of the Red Cross Society of China to appoint me as an honorary director of the plague hospital. Your kindness and concern for relief efforts are greatly appreciated. My talent is limited, and I dare not accept. However, I should do my part for the public welfare of my hometown. I will follow your lead and do my best. I respectfully wish you peace. Niu Yongjian, Minister of the Civil Service, respectfully."

Qingpu

▲ Unfortunate Incident During Bandit Suppression: Zhangliantang, Jinze, Guanwang Temple, Xicen, and other areas in Qingpu County are places where bandits frequently appear, and kidnappings and robberies are common occurrences. There have also been several cases of small boats on the inland river being robbed. To eliminate harm for the people, the Qingpu County Government held a bandit suppression conference in Zhangliantang at 1:00 PM on the 10th of this month and decided to set out in full force that evening to clear the territory of bandits within twenty days. Unexpectedly, at around 7:00 PM that night, Cao Guisheng, a patrolman under Wang Yulin of the County Water Patrol Team, was holding Wang's No. 3546 automatic pistol and suddenly fired a shot at a pedestrian, Wang Jinqian, on the central street of Zhangliantang. Wang was injured and fled into the Gongyimao shop. Cao chased after him and fired two more shots, hitting him in vital areas. Wang immediately collapsed in the second courtyard of the Gongyimao shop. The murderer, seeing that his goal had been achieved, immediately fled. Fortunately, Song Yaozhang, a shop assistant at Gongyimao, followed him and apprehended him in front of the headquarters of the Security Corps. The next morning, the murderer was sent to the county. The county government specially sent investigating officer Shi Wending to the town at noon on the 12th to inspect the body and confirmed that he had been shot twice in vital areas and died. The deceased had a young child who cried loudly on the spot, begging for justice. Those who heard it could not help but shed tears. Since the incident occurred, the citizens of the town have been very angry. Dozens of shops, including Gongyimao, Gongtai, Dianfu, and Fukang, have jointly petitioned the county government, demanding that the murderer in this case be severely punished and that the county government should clearly indicate how the lives of the people will be protected in the future. The district office, the town office, and the local gentry will all express their serious concerns.

▲ Party Department Dispute Escalates: The county party department is being sued by the Anti-Japanese Association and businesses at the provincial party headquarters and provincial government for allegedly mismanaging the anti-Japanese association's funds. Recently, a dispute arose over the re-election of the party departments in districts 1, 2, and 3, with new party members from other areas having improper procedures. The district party departments have accused the county party department of private manipulation of the election and have sent telegrams to the provincial party headquarters requesting investigation and handling.

▲ Blood Soul Anti-Traitor Group Warns Traitorous Merchants: After the establishment of the National Salvation and Anti-Traitor Group in this county, the Blood Soul Anti-Traitor Group was also established. The other day, a silk and foreign goods store in Shaxi was discovered to have secretly imported twenty pieces of direct tribute wool and twenty pieces of twill from enemy countries. A silk and cloth store in the Xishi market of Zhintang was discovered to have secretly imported over three thousand taels of enemy goods. The Blood Soul Anti-Traitor Group learned of this and sent a letter of warning, which stated in essence that the sale of Japanese goods has been increasing in this county recently, and the situation in Rehe and Tianjin is becoming increasingly critical. Driven by conscience and boiling with hot blood, the group had no choice but to warn the store to seal up or even burn all Japanese goods within one week. If future sales of enemy goods are discovered, the group will take the most severe measures. Do not say you were not warned.

The Jingde Department Store on Guanqian Street in Suzhou received a letter from the Anti-Traitor Group, stating that it had heard that the company was secretly selling enemy goods and would take drastic measures if it continued to do so. The next day, it received another letter with similar wording. In addition to sending the original letter to the Public Security Bureau, the company posted a notice at the entrance stating that it did not sell Japanese goods.

▲ Shanghai Party Department Investigates Zheng Ying: Zheng Ying, the Shanghai woman who publicly promoted licentiousness in Suzhou last summer, left Suzhou and returned to Shanghai after the Public Security Bureau ordered her arrest. She recently secretly arrived in Suzhou and is hiding in the Huayuan Hotel. Therefore, officials were sent from Shanghai the other day to Suzhou to join the Wu County Party Department and the Public Security Bureau in sending officials to the Huayuan Hotel to investigate, but she was not there. They are currently conducting a thorough investigation in various hotels.

Wuxi

▲ Resolution of the Small Boat Destruction Case: The Huayu small boat of the Zhonghua Hengyu Shipping Company, which operates between Wuxi and Caohe, was passing by Donggang Bridge near Xindu Bridge the other day when it was suddenly blocked by over a hundred villagers holding yellow stones who had gathered on the bridge. They also smashed the boat and beat the cook, Jiang Hanqing, and others. The troublemaking villager, You Zibing, was brought to the city and sent to the Second Branch of the Public Security Bureau for investigation. It is now learned that the case has been mediated by Qian Chongqing, a local dignitary from Xindu Bridge, who persuaded the people of the town to abide by the law in the future and not to cause trouble lightly. They also offered compensation for the company's losses as a resolution. As for the troublemaker, You Zibing, the Second Branch of the Public Security Bureau leniently sentenced him to detention as punishment. The Huayu small boat, for the convenience of transportation, resumed its regular schedule yesterday.

Changzhou

▲ Security Corps Captures Two Notorious Bandits: The Security Corps of the Fourth District of Wuyi County received a secret report that several notorious bandits who had repeatedly committed kidnapping cases had sneaked back home and were planning to commit a crime in a certain village. Trainer Zhang Yaoqing led the corps members to search at night and captured two notorious bandits, Pei Jinsheng and Tai Rongbao. After interrogation, they confessed to committing multiple kidnapping and extortion cases and were sent to the county for trial on the 15th.

▲ Traitorous Merchants Paraded Through the Streets: Recently, five traitorous merchants, including Diao Guangcai, were found in Benniu Town, Wuyi County, along with three items of enemy goods. Jiangyin

▲ Customs Patrol Boat Seizes Opium: Chen Zhixing, captain of patrol boat No. 3 of the 3rd squadron of the 16th Customs Patrol Team, received a report on the afternoon of the 12th that a Wusong ship was transporting 2,250 taels of opium, which belonged to Yang Lianzi, an opium smuggler from Jingjiang, and Cheng Tiansheng, an opium smuggler from Jiangyin. It was being unloaded at Juegang in Jiangbei. Chen immediately arrived at Juegang at 1:00 AM on the 13th and seized 1,500 taels of opium from Yang Lianzi, totaling sixteen large cakes. Cheng Tiansheng escaped. It is unknown where the opium was taken. Squadron Leader Ling Xichao questioned Chen about it on the 14th, but Chen denied seizing any opium, making it a suspicious case.

▲ Fugitive Dike Worker Arrested and Sent to County: Xu Ruiao, the supervisor of the Laishing'an dike project in Jiangbei, caused a major dike failure due to his negligence. After the provincial government ordered the county to secretly arrest him, he was not found. The fugitive suddenly returned to Danyang yesterday and was discovered by Patrol Officer Zhou of the Third Branch of the Public Security Bureau, who led the police to arrest him on the spot. He has now been sent to the county by the general office.

▲ Traitorous Merchants Arrested in Lucheng: The Danyang County Party Department received a telegram from Jiang Qian of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association in Lucheng Town, stating that seven Jiangbei traitorous merchants, including Jiang Xumao, were carrying various kinds of enemy goods and staying at the Huangjia Inn. After investigation, they were arrested by the association together with the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau and sent to Danyang this afternoon. The county party department has instructed the Anti-Japanese Association to send people to meet and detain them.

▲ Drought and Famine Repeatedly Reported in Northwestern Townships: This county has had little rainfall in recent months, and most of the crops in the fields have withered. County Magistrate Wang has personally gone to the townships to investigate. It is also reported that locusts have appeared in the northern townships, and the county government has ordered the agricultural station to send people to investigate and quickly supervise the farmers to exterminate them.

Yangzhou

▲ One-Week Commemoration of the Grand Canal Breach: According to the Gregorian calendar, the Grand Canal breach last autumn was on August 26th, but most villagers adhere to the lunar calendar, which puts it on July 13th. This year, on the lunar July 13th, the various sectors of Shaobo Town, where the most breaches occurred in this county, initiated a one-week commemoration and memorial service for the compatriots who died in the disaster. It is said that in addition to holding a memorial service that day, high-ranking monks were invited to offer salvation to the souls of those who died unjustly. In the evening, lotus lanterns and paper ingots were released on the Xiangwai two rivers, to commemorate the lonely ghosts who were drowned. When the lanterns were released and the ingots burned, the wailing of the families of the victims on both banks shook the fields, and those who heard it could not help but feel heartbroken. It is a pity that those in charge of the entire Grand Canal project before the breach did not hear this crying and let them examine their hearts. It is also learned that the disaster relief association will still hold a large-scale memorial service on the 26th.

▲ Anti-Japanese Association Seizes Enemy Goods: The Fangyuanxing Yarn Shop on E'gengxiangwan, this city, was found to be secretly selling enemy goods yesterday (14th). A full committee meeting was convened at 3:00 PM today (15th) to discuss how to deal with Fangyuanxing.

Nantong

▲ Banditry Rages Again in Eastern Townships: Recently, there has been another bandit uprising in Yiyu and other areas in the eastern townships of Tongyi County. The situation is very rampant. After the police and militia suppressed them, the bandits resisted stubbornly. Fifteen bandits were captured on the 14th, and seven machine guns and more than ten rifles were seized. They were sent to the county government on the 15th. Upon learning of this, all sectors of the local community were deeply concerned that the horrific situation of the 18th year of the Republic would return. On the 15th, an emergency meeting was held at the Chamber of Commerce, chaired by County Magistrate Zhang Dong, who proposed that the situation in the eastern townships was urgent and that the county government should request Commander Zhu of the provincial security regiment stationed in the city to quickly send a team to Yiyu to suppress the uprising. It was decided to recommend Gu Zuoqing and Shen Shaochang to go to the regiment headquarters to contact him. Commander Zhu immediately dispatched a team to suppress the bandits.

▲ Estimated Cotton Harvest in Tongzhou: According to the county agricultural station, the area of cotton fields in Nantong this year is estimated to be about 1,189,000 mu, accounting for 45% of the county's area, a decrease of one-tenth compared to last year. The current cotton crop is still good, and the estimated cotton yield is an average of 60 jin of seed cotton per mu, with a total of about 710,000 dan for the county.

▲ Searching for Drifting Soldiers and Scattered Braves: All armed groups in Nantong held a meeting on the 15th, convened by Commander Zhu of the provincial security regiment, and decided to form a patrol team to search for drifting soldiers and scattered braves.

Rugao

▲ Long Drought, No Rain, Blessed with Timely Rain: This county has not had rain for months since the beginning of summer. The rivers are dry, and the crops are withering. On the afternoon of the 12th, there was a sudden downpour, and the weather suddenly became cooler. Although it was very short, the people's hearts were greatly comforted.

▲ Penniless, Hanged Himself in a Shed: Zheng Fuyuan, a farmer in Guba Town, had previously borrowed 14 yuan from Liu Kunxiang. Because Liu was urging him to repay the debt and Zheng was unable to do so, Zheng, in a moment of desperation, went to Liu's shed at night on the 11th and hanged himself.

Jiaxing

▲ Homicide Occurs in Daqiao Township: Yao Zou, the wife of Yao A'er, a farmer in Zhijiabang, Daqiao Township, Jiaxing, had an affair with her neighbor Zhu A'san. On the 7th of this month, A'er was beaten by the adulterer, and then beaten again by the adulterer's father, Zhu A'da. A'er suddenly disappeared. On the 10th, A'er's torn clothes and shoes were found on the bank of the river in Bangnei. After a search by people in the river, A'er's body was found. The two murderers immediately fled. The branch office ordered the police to arrest Yao Zou and Zhu A'san's mother and bring them to the bureau. As the case is a major homicide, it has been reported to the local branch court for an autopsy. Meanwhile, the main criminals are being strictly pursued for investigation and prosecution.

Ningbo

▲ Unprecedented Fire in Cicheng: The Guzhu Paper Shop between Zhuxiangkou and Shixingkou in Cixi City caught fire on the evening of the 12th. Because the manager, Shao, was out, the shop assistants locked the shop door and went upstairs to gamble. Later, a customer wanted to buy something from the shop and saw that the door was locked, so he knocked on the door. The apprentices upstairs heard the sound and thought the manager had returned to the shop, so they rushed to clean up the gambling equipment, accidentally knocking over a Mobil lamp, which burned the paper materials on the ground. The fire immediately raged, bursting through the roof and spreading rapidly. It burned for four hours from 11:00 PM on the 12th to 3:00 AM the next morning before it was extinguished. A total of more than 200 street houses were burned down. The victims included more than 30 stores, including Guzhu Paper Shop, Tianzhang Hat Shop, Shendacheng Fruit Shop, Rongzhangxiang Silk Shop, Baoyuan Silver Shop, Baoyu Silver Shop, Mobil Oil Company, Chunhuaxiang Silk and Foreign Goods Advertising, Chengzhang Silk and Foreign Goods Shop, Taichang South Goods, and Demao Oil Candle, with losses of more than 500,000 yuan. It was truly an unprecedented fire in Cicheng.

▲ Tragedy Occurs While Watching a Play on a Stage: Shen Yingxiang, a resident of Wucheyan, Yuyao, is over sixty years old. He used to be the manager of the Zhihe Money Shop in Shanghai and was well-known in the business community. Later, because Zhihe went bankrupt, he returned to his native Wuche for residence. On the evening of the 12th of this month, because Wucheyan was putting on a ghost opera, the stage was conveniently located in front of Shen's house. Yingxiang ordered the servants to build a stage in front of the door to watch the play. At about 10:00 PM, a man speaking with a Shanghai accent squeezed onto Yingxiang's stage. After clarifying that it was Yingxiang, he drew a pistol and fired at him. At that time, Yingxiang's second daughter had also returned to Ningbo to watch the play and was next to her father. Fearing that her father would be kidnapped by the thugs, she quickly hugged her father with both hands. Unexpectedly, the man shot her second daughter. Both father and daughter were hit by a bullet. Yingxiang's second son, Shanfu, heard the gunshot in the house and went outside to ask. Five or six thugs suddenly appeared and fired at Shanfu, who immediately fell to the ground and died shortly after. At this time, a farmer from the Linshan Lake dike, someone named Jia, was also watching the play and looked at the thugs after seeing Shanfu fall to the ground. The thugs shot at Jia, hitting a vital spot, and he also died on the spot. Three of Yingxiang's servants were also wounded by the thugs with guns. After the thugs shot down Yingxiang and others, they fled one after another.

First Day of the National Sports Conference

▲ Opening Ceremony Held in the Morning, Followed by the First General Assembly

▲ Section Reviews in the Afternoon, Zhu Jia-hua Hosts Banquet for Members in the Evening

The Lowest Hopes for the National Sports Conference ·Hao Gengsheng·

Physical education has long been a focus of national defense in the East and West, and has been particularly emphasized since the European War. It is an important part of the entire educational process and is of great importance to the nation's vitality and national spirit. However, successive rulers in our country have not paid attention to it. Today, the national situation is becoming increasingly weak, which is largely due to the failure of politics, economics, and the entire education system to be on the right track. However, the lack of physical strength and the lack of energy among the general population are also major factors. Today, the government, in the midst of a serious national crisis, has convened the National Sports Conference to plan the implementation of national sports, which is a very good intention. However, this conference is a new event in the history of our country, and its nature is for open national discussion, so there will be many proposals and the scope will be broad. With a little carelessness, the result of the discussion will inevitably repeat the mistakes of general conferences, with trivial details being emphasized and the fundamental issues being ignored. I believe that to avoid this, the proposals at this conference should be broadly divided into two groups:

(1) Research Aspect - relating to curriculum, teaching materials, testing, investigation, and personnel training, etc.

(2) Administrative Aspect - relating to facilities, organization, meetings, inspections, and international competitions, etc.

The above two points should be regarded as the general outline for the research of this conference. According to this general outline, although there are many proposals, they can be integrated and connected, and will not interfere with each other, so that the researchers can calmly recognize their true value, and the future implementation of each proposal after it is passed can also be promoted accordingly to achieve success. Now, I would like to express my lowest hope for this conference based on this general outline:

(1) The government should carefully select one or two academic institutions or organizations with more history and better performance, designate them as national sports research centers, and sponsor them to broadly recruit sports scholars from home and abroad, conduct in-depth research based on modern science and great historical background, and find ways to solve all current sports problems, so that national sports administrators have something to follow.

(2) Under the central administrative system of the government, a national sports administrative general agency should be established, and sports administrative talents from home and abroad should be widely recruited (the number should not be large, but it must fully implement the established plan), cooperate and connect with local sports agencies and sports, and promote the plans decided by the central government based on the findings of the researchers. If so, then the scattered national sports can gradually get on the right track, and the gains from this conference, at a minimum, can lay a more systematic foundation for national sports facilities.

Zhu Jiahua presided over the meeting, and Shi Wei served as the master of ceremonies. First, Zhu gave the opening speech. At 9:15, Peng Xuepei finished his speech, and they took a photo first and then continued the meeting. Chu Minyi presided over the meeting and reported on the preparations. After a rest at 10:00, the first general meeting was held. The speeches of each person and the situation of the first general meeting are recorded as follows:

Zhu Jiahua's Opening Speech

▲The Motivation and Preparation Process of the Conference

▲Significant Contributions to School Physical Education

▲Future Education Should Strive to Promote Physical Education

▲Promoting Physical Education Requires Universal Development

Opening speech by Zhu Jiahua, Minister of Education and Chairman of the Conference:

Central Committee members, representatives of various ministries, representatives from various regions, esteemed physical education experts, today marks the inaugural National Physical Education Conference held in the capital. I am deeply honored by your presence. This conference is a pioneering event in China, the result of a long period of deliberation. Back in July of the eighteenth year [of the Republic], the West Lake Exposition initiated the National Games. At that time, the Ministry of Education planned to convene a national physical education conference and appointed Mr. Chu Minyi as the director of preparations. Originally scheduled to coincide with the National Games in Hangzhou in September, the conference was postponed due to the postponement of the Games. The Ministry of Education also convened the Second National Education Conference at this time, making it difficult to attend to both. Furthermore, Mr. Chu Minyi was traveling to Belgium to attend the Universal Exposition commemorating the centennial of Belgian independence, which prevented the conference from taking place. The outbreak of national crisis has further exposed the physical weaknesses of the Chinese people, and it is widely recognized that promoting national physical education is essential to revitalize the national spirit. The Ministry, recognizing this urgency, convened the First National Physical Education Conference. We initially set the standards for membership and the number of participants, along with a budget, which was approved by the Executive Yuan. Today marks the opening ceremony. The conference regulations and the organizational outline of the preparatory committee were previously promulgated by the Ministry, and we appointed members to the preparatory committee, including Mr. Chu Minyi as the director, to actively prepare. This is the history of the conference's preparation and establishment.

The members attending this conference include the directors of physical education from national, provincial, and registered private universities or independent colleges, physical education instructors or heads of public sports fields selected by provincial and municipal education departments, principals of national, provincial, municipal, and registered private physical education colleges, directors of national martial arts institutes from the central government and various provinces and cities, physical education experts invited by the Ministry of Education, and representatives from various ministries and commissions. We have brought together administrative personnel and physical education experts to jointly promote national education, discuss physical education implementation plans, unify training guidelines, and foster the physical development, fitness, and strength of the people, as well as improve national health and revitalize the national spirit. Its significance and mission are of great importance. In addition to the draft implementation plan for national physical education drafted by experts Wu Yunrui, Yuan Dunli, and Hao Gengsheng, who were previously appointed by the Ministry of Education, the conference will also discuss over 200 proposals received from members. After careful deliberation by all members, various resolutions will be passed and either promulgated and implemented by the Ministry of Education or forwarded to relevant agencies for reference. This will undoubtedly make a significant contribution to school physical education in the future, which is the first thing I must report to everyone.

Physical education occupies an extremely important position in education. We know that education is not merely about imparting knowledge. The purpose of modern education is, on the one hand, to train individuals in the overall functioning of their bodies to aid their growth, and on the other hand, to ensure that individuals, with their healthy bodies, can adapt to the demands of social evolution. While there is more than one educational method, their function is to achieve the aforementioned goals. Modern philosophy, psychology, and biology all recognize the close relationship between the human body and mind. Although physical education involves the movement of large muscles in the human body to aid physical development and enhance health, its effects must lead to psychological changes through physiological changes. Therefore, physical education is closely related to intellectual, moral, aesthetic, and physical development. The common failings of Chinese education today are, on the one hand, the inability to cultivate practical talents for the production sector, and on the other hand, the inability to cultivate loyal, courageous, and aspiring citizens. The insult of being called the "sick man of East Asia" has yet to be erased. The reason lies in what is self-evident. We, who strive for education, should recognize the environment and never blindly copy. What China needs today is education that promotes production and education that revitalizes the national spirit. In terms of revitalizing the national spirit, it is not something that can be achieved merely through slogans and declarations. We must do our best to develop the physical fitness, ability, and strength of the people to create loyal, courageous, and aspiring citizens, and then we can revitalize the national spirit. In the past, physical education in Chinese education was seriously lacking. Although school education had formal physical education courses, due to the lack of talent, insufficient funding, and methods that were not fully appropriate, it contributed very little to youth physical education. As for national physical education in social education, it is still in its infancy. We are heartbroken by the national crisis and look to the future, asking how we can make a tremendous determination to eliminate the accumulated problems in education and open up new opportunities for future education. This is what those engaged in education today should strive for together.

Another point is that the purpose of promoting physical education is to enable the physical fitness, ability, and strength of all Chinese people to develop universally in order to revitalize the national spirit. However, those who are ignorant fail to see this and only focus on sports meets and athletic associations in various places, emphasizing competition in the skills of a small number of people, as if only promoting an abnormality without universal implications. They also believe that these few people often do not study other subjects or engage in other occupations besides physical education. Therefore, people generally harbor doubts and do not pay attention to it. They do not know that at a time when school physical education and national physical education in China have not yet developed, we need these few people to devote all their efforts to it, just like revolutionary work. There is no reward without sacrifice. We can even say that these few people are the sacrificers in the period of promoting physical education. This conference will inevitably be heard and doubted by society, or even dismissed as an unimportant matter during the national crisis. This must be explained to the outside world first.

Zhu Jiahua's opening speech (photographed by Guanghua, Nanjing)

The conference is scheduled for only five days, and time is extremely pressing. I hope that all members will pay attention to time economy and strive to avoid any vague theories or unimportant disputes. As for the members and experts who have come from afar to participate in this unprecedented event, I would like to express my deep gratitude on behalf of the Ministry. How to realize the Ministry's hope in convening this conference will depend on all the representatives and experts. I wish you all success in our joint efforts.

▲Reporting on the Preparations

Chu Minyi, Director of the Preparatory Committee, reported on the preparations in great detail, describing the origins of the conference, the organization of the Preparatory Committee, the preparation process, the appointment of experts, the conference venue and reception, and funding, etc. As reported by Peng Baichuan and Guo Lianfeng in yesterday's newspaper, there are only minor differences, so I will not repeat them.

Chen Lifu's Instructions from the Central Party Headquarters Representative

▲Integrate the National Spirit with Chinese and Western Physical Education

▲Formulate a Plan Suitable for the Economic Environment

▲Develop Physical Education in a Simple Way

▲For National Survival, There Must Be Physical Creation

▲The Results of the Conference Should Be Implemented Earnestly

Today, I am very honored to participate in this grand event. The chairman has spoken in great detail about the significance of the conference. What I will say is only a small amount, merely to supplement his remarks.

I have heard that in addition to the implementation plan for national physical education drafted by specially appointed experts, over 200 proposals have been received. Among them, there must be many valuable proposals. In recent years, there have been two contradictory phenomena in Chinese academic circles: on the one hand, there is a strong effort to promote Chinese national essence and oppose foreign culture, and on the other hand, there is an absolute worship of Western culture and opposition to inherent Chinese things. These two contradictory phenomena are very obvious in medicine, art, and physical education. Both are wrong. If we study Mr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings, we see that his efforts in the revolution were to seek survival for the nation and freedom and equality for the country. He paid close attention to the promotion of national self-confidence. National self-confidence means not belittling oneself on the one hand, and not being arrogantly self-aggrandizing on the other. The meaning is very profound. There are many reasons for the decline of the Chinese nation, physical education being one of them, while the shallowness of knowledge and the decline of morality also have an indirect impact. If we want to solve the problem of physical education in China, we should not only seek it in a narrow sense. What Mr. Sun Yat-sen told us, we should know what to uphold in order to resolve this contradictory phenomenon. Cultural conflict and contradictory phenomena are unavoidable in the course of cultural development, and it is our responsibility to resolve these contradictory phenomena. This is what I would like to ask all experts and representatives to pay attention to. China has always attached importance to physical education, but its methods are different from what is being promoted now. We should seek to promote it on the basis of not belittling ourselves and not being arrogantly self-aggrandizing. All Chinese academic and cultural fields should seek solutions on the same basis, including medicine, art, and physical education.

Today, I saw Mr. Chu Minyi's article. Mr. Chu's point of view is based on French and Italian taijiquan movements. I would also like to ask Mr. Zhang Zhijiang, who emphasizes national martial arts movements, to note that national martial arts movements and physical education are parallel and not contradictory. We feel that Western sports are suitable for group life, and through group life, group sports occur, and from group sports, the moral and intellectual education of the people is developed. This kind of sport is suitable for urban life. Most Chinese people live in rural areas and enjoy the beauty of nature. From my personal observation, these economic conditions are very important. For example, in the case of playing tennis, the tennis racket alone costs more than six yuan, and the tennis ball costs several yuan, so it costs at least a dozen yuan to play. If economic conditions cannot be solved, physical education can only be exclusive to schools and can only be enjoyed by the bourgeoisie. How can we make valuable things cheaper and complex things simpler, so that sports are not unique to urban areas but are popularized in rural areas, and seek progress in physical education in ordinary ways? This is also what I hope will be noted at the conference.

A country and a nation can stand in the world only if they have unique qualities. It is a disgrace that we are good at physical education but only know how to imitate and cannot create. Under the current economic conditions in China, it is very necessary to invent a new sport to express the national spirit. This is also what I hope the conference will pay attention to and resolve. For example, English football and American baseball are popular all over the country and can well express the national spirit of their countries. In China, which practices the Three Principles of the People, how should we create new physical education sports to promote the Chinese national spirit? It seems that this is a valuable issue to pay attention to. A month ago, the Chinese representatives were completely defeated at the World Games. This is not shameful. What is shameful is that there is no creation or promotion of the national spirit. Independent creation. Great Chinese people should create a sport for people from other countries to imitate. We should not specialize in following in the footsteps of foreigners. This is the expression of the spirit of national self-confidence. I hope everyone at the conference will pay attention to this.

Furthermore, physical education is not something that can be achieved with mere empty words. We should move from knowing to doing. After everyone has formulated a good implementation plan, we should work hard to promote it, spread it throughout the country, and seek practical results. This is also what I hope from all the gentlemen at the conference.

In summary, what I, representing the central government, hope from the conference is: First, to integrate the strengths of Chinese and Western physical education with the spirit of national self-confidence, not belittling oneself or being arrogantly self-aggrandizing, and to formulate a plan suitable for the economic environment in China; Second, to develop physical education in an ordinary and simple way; Third, in order to seek national survival, we must have great creations to contribute to the world and build a unique new physical education plan for the Chinese nation; Fourth, from today onwards, we hope that the results of the National Physical Education Conference will be earnestly implemented.

He Yingqin's Speech on Behalf of the National Government

▲Formulate a Universal Plan Suitable for National Conditions

▲Eliminate Bad Habits that Hinder Physical Education

▲The Formulated Plan Should Be Simple and Practical

Today, I am very honored to represent the National Government and say a few words at the National Physical Education Conference. The World Games have just concluded in Los Angeles, USA. All the larger countries in the world had representatives in attendance, and they were all able to showcase their unique strengths. The Chinese delegation only had two representatives, and they did not even make it to the finals. This shows that the Chinese nation has always not paid attention to physical education, and this has reached an extreme. Originally, the purpose of physical education was not to win medals, but sports are a type of physical education that has the effect of increasing physical and mental strength. In ancient Chinese education, rites, music, archery, charioteering, writing, and arithmetic were called the six arts, and archery was a matter of physical education. Schools were established to teach it, but later generations did not pay attention to it and became increasingly degenerate. If we want to seek the revival of the Chinese nation, there are many methods, but it can be said that we should start with physical education.

Mr. Chen said just now that Chinese people have two contradictory phenomena: on the one hand, they preserve the national essence, and on the other hand, they admire Western culture. Both are biased. I hope that all representatives and experts will pay attention to this. Chinese martial arts and various foreign sports each have their own strengths and weaknesses. For example, they emphasize aesthetics and the development of only a part of the body. Gymnastics in various countries is almost focused on the fingers, or on the limbs, all of which are shortcomings.

Formulating a plan that integrates Chinese and Western physical education is what I hope from the conference. Chinese martial arts focus on individual sports, and there are very few that implement team sports. This shortcoming should be supplemented, and efforts should be made to make national physical education disciplined and universal. The formulation of this plan is what I hope from all the gentlemen.

Secondly, we must eliminate bad habits and bad addictions. These have a huge impact on Chinese physical education. We must eliminate the bad habits of young people, such as smoking, drinking, and gambling. Students in Chinese schools at all levels are unwilling to wear shorts, and women in remote villages still have bound feet. Women in cities do not bind their feet, but they bind their breasts, all of which hinder physical development. The prohibition of these negative aspects is also what I hope the conference will pay attention to. In the neighboring country of Japan, two or thirty years ago, people were short and small, and they were ashamed of it. They paid attention to the promotion of physical education and the elimination of bad habits. Male and female students are required to wear shorts. As a result, the height of the people in their country has increased year by year. In the past thirty years, the average increase has been one inch. This is related to physical development. I hope the conference will pay attention to this.

Since the National Government established its capital, many conferences have been held, and there have been many conference proposals. The spirit is very good, but they end up being put on the shelf. This is the first time for a plenary conference on matters related to national survival. It is very important. I hope that everyone will formulate a simple and practical plan that is in line with economic conditions and other factors. A plan, no matter how good, is useless if it cannot be implemented. This plan should also be permanent. We should strive for it to be discussed and feasible. When I was in the Training Supervision Department, I formulated a military education plan, but although the government issued an order for its implementation, very few were able to actually implement it. After the conference is over, how can we supervise and promote its implementation? I hope everyone will pay attention to this. There are very few physical education instructors in China. I personally want to run a model physical education school in the central government, and the gentlemen also have this proposal. I hope it can be put into practice.

Today, I have said a total of three points: First, to formulate a universal physical education plan suitable for national conditions; Second, to eliminate bad habits that hinder physical education; Third, to formulate a simple and feasible plan. That's all.

Photograph of all the guests and members (photographed by Guanghua, Nanjing)

Peng Xuepei's Speech on Behalf of the Executive Yuan

▲Chinese Physical Education is Heading Towards Suicide

▲Promotion Requires Universal Facilities Like Mahjong

Today, I represent the Executive Yuan in welcoming everyone. Just now, I heard Mr. He Jingzhi say that the Japanese in the neighboring country are short, and their achievements in the World Games are very good. We feel very ashamed. I say that shame is not limited to this. There is something even more shameful, such as the spread of cholera, which is only prevalent in China. This is due to the lack of physical education knowledge among the Chinese people. Chinese people harm their bodies every day and head towards suicide every day. For example, they are unwilling to get vaccinations that cost very little, but they have to buy coffins that cost dozens of yuan. It is very hateful. The need to pay attention to physical education knowledge is the most urgent task today. Chinese people often do not pay attention to physical education after leaving school until they reach the age of thirty. Mr. Chen Lifu said that economic conditions are certainly a major reason, but the lack of active promotion is also a reason. Chinese people usually do not pay attention to various physical education sports, but there are also those who pay attention, namely mahjong. That is why I think that if someone promotes various physical education sports and the facilities for physical education venues throughout the country are as widespread as mahjong, then physical education will naturally develop. In addition, there should be enthusiastic physical educators who practice it and promote it. This is what I hope the gentlemen at the conference will vigorously promote.

—Record of the First General Assembly—

▲Zhang Zhijiang Elected as Vice President

—Yuan Dunli Reports on the Draft Plan

Yesterday morning, after the opening ceremony, the first general assembly commenced at 10:00 AM. A total of 107 members were present. Chu Minyi served as chairman, and Zhang Wei Gao and Huang Wenqi served as recorders. The proceedings were conducted with due formality.

(1) Determining Member Seating

The assigned seating numbers ranged from number 10 to number 121.

(2) Election of Vice Speaker

Zhang Zhijiang was elected as Vice Speaker with 29 votes. The next highest vote counts were as follows: Yuan Dunli with 25 votes; Hao Gengsheng and Shao Rugan each with 15 votes; Wu Yunrui, Zhang Xinfu, Jin Zhaojun, Du Tingxiu, and Wu Bangwei each receiving 2 votes; and 14 others receiving 1 vote each.

(3) Report by Yuan Dunli

Mr. Yuan reported on the process of drafting the "National Physical Education Implementation Plan" as follows:

The Ministry of Education appointed myself and Messrs. Hao Gengsheng and Wu Yunrui to compile this draft, a decision made during the preparatory meeting on June 17th. The draft was completed before July 1st. As the three of us were in Beiping at the time, we also invited figures from the northern sports community to discuss it together. By August 1st, it was sent to the Ministry of Education. Regarding the content, the first section, the introduction, is based on understanding the question of what physical education is, which is very important. The second, objectives, sets the direction. The third, administration and facilities, takes into account that China's physical education administrative system is not as complete as that of European and American countries, and this chapter particularly focuses on this point in order to improve it. The fourth, methods of promoting physical education, emphasizes five points: (1) research work, (2) cultivation of talent, (3) standards for physical education implementation, (4) promotion and encouragement of various physical education gatherings and organizations, (5) methods for evaluating physical education achievements. The fifth, a phased implementation plan, is necessary because the proposed plan cannot be fully implemented all at once and must be phased in. The drafted plan still has many omissions. It is hoped that the results obtained from this meeting will be appropriately supplemented into this plan to strive for perfection. Also, when the review committee convenes, although it will be divided into five groups, everyone is requested to, on the one hand, base their efforts on the essence of the proposals and, on the other hand, incorporate them into the implementation plan so that ideals and reality can coexist without contradiction. Furthermore, although the three of us are nominally responsible for drafting this plan, there are actually many educators and physical educators helping out. I especially wish to express my gratitude.

Review Committee Meeting Reports

(1) First Meeting of the Objectives Group

▲Balanced Development of All Aspects of Personality

—Promoting Healthy Beauty—

Nanjing, 16th: Members of the first group, the Physical Education Objectives group, including Wu Zhimin and others, elected Wu as chairman, and Shang Shujing as secretary. (1) Regarding the proposal to use education, science, popularization, life, play, and naturalization as the six main objectives for national physical education, it was resolved to send it to the research group for discussion as a basis for selecting teaching materials, standards, and principles. (2) Regarding the proposal to earnestly promote the balanced development of all aspects of personality, it was resolved that the original proposal be adopted. The word "balanced" will be added to the first item, i.e., to provide citizens with ample opportunities for balanced physical development. (3) Regarding the proposal to define the national physical education policy, it was resolved that the proposed sections will be adopted, as they have already been mentioned in the implementation plan of this association. The (cultivating citizens' morality) in the rationale of the original proposal and the (focusing on moral cultivation) in the methods will be adopted into the objectives. (4) Regarding the proposal that school physical education should focus on the widespread improvement of the health of all students, it was resolved that the rationale of the original proposal has already been mentioned in the plan. Regarding the methods, it will be sent to the evaluation group for review. (5) Regarding the proposal to draft a national physical education plan to be jointly observed based on the international situation, the current national situation, physical education trends, and national physique, it was resolved that the proposed methods were not detailed, so the review will be postponed. (6) Regarding the proposal to promote traditional Chinese martial arts, it was resolved that the rationale of the original proposal will be incorporated into the fourth item of the plan's objectives. (7) Regarding the proposal to promote healthy beauty, it was resolved to incorporate it into the objectives of the plan.

(2) First Meeting of the Administrative Organization Group

▲Proposals to be Organized and Discussed

Nanjing, 16th: Yuan Dunli as chairman, Wu Bangwei as secretary of the second group. 1. The review method is to review each proposal of this group one by one. Those that should be merged will be merged for review, those that should be amended will have opinions put forward and submitted to the meeting for discussion, and those that should be retained will be retained. 2. Lu Song'en, Zhang Zhijiang, and Chen Baiqing were nominated to be responsible for organizing the proposals, submitting them to this group for discussion, and reporting to the third general assembly.

(3) First Meeting of the Research Group

▲School Sports Technical Standards Passed

Nanjing, 16th: Fifteen members of the third group, Physical Education Research, were present. Chu Minyi chaired, Feng Shunnan recorded. Resolved: 1. There are eighteen proposals in the general catalog. According to their nature, they were divided and merged into a total of nine proposals. Proposal No. 8 was sent to the fourth group for review. 2. The first and second proposals were passed in principle and submitted to the general assembly to discuss the methods. They will be reserved for future central specialized physical education research institutions to implement concretely. 3. Physical education specialty schools were passed in principle. 4. The regulations on school sports technical standards were passed in principle. 5. For the fifth and sixth proposals, Du Longyuan and Xie Siyan were asked to supplement their opinions and revise them. 6. The first proposal from the teacher training group, to first establish a physical education research institute by utilizing secondary school sports, was originally passed and submitted to the general assembly.

(4) First Meeting of the Implementation and Promotion Group

▲Divided into Three Subgroups: Teacher Training, Military Training, and Public Physical Education and Children's Physical Education

Nanjing, 16th: The fourth group's review committee is discussing various implementation and promotion proposals. Chairman Peng. It was resolved that this group covers too much and should be divided into three subgroups for review: (1) Teacher training, including teacher continuing education, overseas study qualifications, and treatment; (2) Military training, including military sports; (3) Public physical education and children's physical education. The above three subgroups will each have a limit of seven people, but the review results will be reported to the entire group and then reported to the general assembly. The first subgroup included Wu Tong, Liu Changhe, Jin Zhaojun, Peng Baichuan, Xu Minhui, Sun Mingxiu, Li Jiyuan, Yu Ziyu, and Zhu Chongming. Chairman Xu was elected, and Sun recorded. Resolved: (1) Teacher training is divided into three major categories: A. Traditional Chinese Martial Arts, B. Physical Education Schools, C. Other. (2) The proposal to select teachers and unify teaching materials for popularizing traditional Chinese martial arts will be merged into the teacher training group. (3) Merge into the Research Group for discussion. (3) The proposal to prepare for the establishment of a national central martial arts specialty school, cultivate talents widely, popularize martial arts to defend the nation, and establish a national specialty school with the definition of Chinese New Martial Arts as Chinese-style sports, will be submitted jointly. The third subgroup, Public Physical Education and Children's Physical Education, Chairman Dong Shouyi, Recorder Wu Geng. Resolved: There are a total of twenty-three proposals for public physical education, divided into three categories: (1) Each province, city, and county should establish public sports fields; (2) Promote public physical education. For the above two proposals, one person will be nominated for each proposal to summarize the opinions of each proposal into a general proposal. Wang Zhuangfei was nominated as the drafter for the establishment of sports fields, and Wang Geng was nominated as the drafter for the promotion of public physical education. Children's physical education will be merged into the Promotion of Physical Education Association.

(5) First Meeting of the Evaluation and Other Groups

▲Implementation of Physical Education Standards Passed in Principle

Nanjing, 16th: The fifth group elected Wu Surui as chairman and Jiang Zhonglingxiu as secretary. Resolved: (1) The proposal that evaluation of physical education achievements should focus on testing was passed in principle. (2) The proposal to reward national physical education was sent to the Implementation and Promotion Group for review. (3) The proposal to reward guidance for public physical education was sent to the Administrative Group. (4) The proposal to strictly implement physical education standards, that students at all levels who fail physical education should not be allowed to graduate, and the proposal to request the Ministry of Education to order schools not to allow students who fail physical education to advance or graduate, were merged into one proposal: strictly implement physical education standards. (5) The proposal to request the Examination Yuan to include physical education technology as a required subject in the examination to facilitate promotion and strengthen civil rights was passed in principle.

Nanjing, 16th: At 4:20 PM on the 16th, all members of the conference took eight cars from the Lizhi Society to pay respects at the Sun Yat-sen Mausoleum. Zhu Jiahua Hosts Banquet for Members

—Yuan Dunli's Reply—

Nanjing, 16th: On the evening of the 16th, Zhu Jiahua hosted a banquet for all members at the Lizhi Society. Guests including Wu Zhihui, He Yingqin, and Peng Xuepei, as well as all members, attended. After a few rounds of drinks, Zhu said, "Although there are no statistics on the weakness and mortality rate of the Chinese nation, it is generally less than forty years old, while in the UK and the US it is around fifty. Therefore, if we want to revive the nation, we must pay attention to the universal development of the nation's physique. Everyone has come from afar, braving the heat, to create a physical education plan suitable for the Chinese nation, which is indeed a precursor to the nation's revival." Yuan Dunli then replied, saying that the government, in order to fundamentally develop national physical education, invited physical education experts and experienced physical education associations to Nanjing to discuss and promote the national physical education plan, changing the government's long-standing policy of promoting it only on paper. This is truly the brightest thing in the history of Chinese physical education. He expressed his gratitude for the excellent hospitality extended to the attendees and felt unworthy of it. Wu Zhihui spoke about the harmony of physical education, considering the problems of food and lodging; being able to eat and sleep, and having a healthy physique, can ensure peace of mind. Ma Liang added that physical education includes the five characters of eating, drinking, defecating, urinating, and sleeping, which can encompass everything. Finally, Chu Minyi reported that the review of each group has been largely completed. The general assembly on the morning of the 17th will hear reports from each group on the review results and submit them to the general assembly for discussion. He then reported on the schedule of public banquets hosted by various organizations, and the meeting adjourned at 9:00 PM.

Yesterday's Provisional Proposals

Government Agency Personnel Must Undergo Physical Examination

Ma Xunbo and others proposed that all levels of government agencies nationwide should conduct physical examinations for personnel employed in the future as a model for national physical education. The plan for this proposal is as follows: (1) Establish unified standards, conduct strict examinations to determine acceptance; (2) The central government orders all levels of agencies to implement it conscientiously. Snippets from the Conference Venue

▲The Detestable Airplane

The venue is close to the airport, and airplanes taking off and landing must pass over the roof of the meeting hall. The sound of the engines is deafening and annoying. During the opening ceremony yesterday, Chen Lifu, He Yingqin, and others were interrupted several times by airplanes while giving speeches. The entire venue was silent, and it took several minutes before they could continue. All the members found the airplanes detestable.

▲Special Paper Fans

The weather is hot, and the venue lacks electric fans. Yesterday, attendees were constantly fanning themselves, mostly with paper fans. Hao Gengsheng held a palm-leaf fan, while a certain martial arts expert used a Kongming-style goose feather fan. Those who did not bring fans used the conference daily or the special publication of the Diligence Bookstore as fans, which were special paper fans.

▲Artistic Slogans

There are only four slogans in the venue: (1) Strengthen the body and the race; (2) Physical education saves the nation; (3) Establish oneself and others; (4) Revolutionize the self and the heart. Each slogan is surrounded by colorful floral borders, making them beautiful and pleasing to the eye. In addition, the Lizhi Society's ten principles of abstinence slogans are hung high on the wall. No one smoked during the many hours of the meeting, which is also influenced by the ten principles of abstinence.

▲Clothing Statistics

Among the 103 members who attended the opening ceremony, apart from four in military uniform, five women, and one in student uniform, 63 were wearing Western suits and 29 were wearing traditional Chinese gowns.

All Sorts of Conference Items

▲Yu Binqi Requests Attention to Swimming

Yu Binqi, Wang Jianxin, Hong Zunsan, and Wu Boqing, who are passionate about swimming, suggest that the National Physical Education Conference pay attention to the promotion of swimming, given the immaturity of swimming in China and the value of swimming.
