Local News

Wang Jingwei and Song Ziwen Return to Beijing by Plane This Morning

Wang Will Go to Lushan After Attending the Central Political Conference

Cai Yuanpei Expresses Determination Not to Assume the Position of President of the Executive Yuan

Since the Standing Committee's discussion meeting a few days ago proposed a solution to Wang Jingwei and Zhang Xueliang's resignations, the rapidly changing political situation seems to have come to an end. Wang is scheduled to take a plane to Beijing with Song Ziwen at six o'clock this morning to attend the Central Political Conference and report the reasons for his resignation, then proceed to Lushan to meet with Lin and Jiang. The details are recorded as follows:

▲ Guests Visiting Wang Jingwei Mr. Wang Jingwei seemed to be staying at his residence on West Pubushi Road the night before. At 8:20 in the morning, Gu Mengyu, Minister of Railways, arrived in Shanghai from Beijing and went straight to Wang's residence to meet with him. At 9:30, Tang Youren, Secretary-General of the Central Political Conference, also arrived. Gu and Tang left together at 10:50. Shortly after, Wang, accompanied by his wife Ms. Chen Bijun, left the residence in car number 778. It was said that they were visiting Mr. Cai Yuanpei. Wang did not return to his residence until after 2:00 PM. At 3:00 PM, former Minister of Transportation Chen Mingshu and Chief of Training Li Jishen came to visit and talked for an hour, leaving together at 4:15. Shortly after, Tang Youren returned to Wang's residence and left after a short while.

▲ Wang Meets with Cai Yuanpei A reporter from the Guowen News Agency met with Wang when he went out to visit Cai. According to his statement to the reporter, "I am going out at this time to visit Mr. Cai Zimin and discuss the successor to the position of President of the Executive Yuan. I am asking Cai to take on the difficult task, and I am determined not to resume the position of President of the Executive Yuan." However, the reporter followed to Cai's residence and the Academia Sinica, but Wang did not go to either place. Later, Wang met with Mr. Cai in the evening.

▲ Chen and Li Visit Wang Yesterday afternoon at 3:30, Chen Mingshu and Li Jishen went to West Pubushi Road to visit Wang, talking until 4:15 before leaving together. A reporter from the Guowen News Agency asked Chen when he would be going abroad, and he replied that he was not going. He continued, "The visit to Wang was just a casual meeting, nothing important." Then, when asked about Li's departure date for Beijing, he replied that it was not yet determined. "Mr. Wang is returning to Beijing tonight, but I (Li referring to himself) am not going with him." The content of Chen and Li's meeting with Wang seemed inconvenient to disclose. After the reporter finished talking, they hurriedly got into a car and returned to their residence separately. Later, according to news from Wang's residence, the conversation between Chen and Li mainly concerned Wang's trip to Lushan and the issue of the successor to the position of President of the Executive Yuan, which was discussed casually and was not of great importance.

▲ Conversation with a Certain Central Committee Member Regarding Wang's return to Beijing, according to a certain Central Committee member, it has been agreed upon, but the matter of resuming the position of President of the Executive Yuan is still under discussion. Regarding the so-called revision of the government organization, some Central Committee members strongly advocated expanding the powers of the Executive Yuan at the Fourth National Congress, making it superior to the other Yuan, so that the President of the Executive Yuan would have the nature of a responsible cabinet, which is the current system. Now it is heard that some Central Committee members have recently advocated reducing the powers of the Executive Yuan and restoring the organization before the Fourth National Congress, completely entrusting political power to the Central Political Conference, and the powers of the five Yuan would be completely subject to the control of the Political Conference. In this case, Wang, as one of the three Standing Committee members, can still develop his ambitions upon returning to Beijing. In the future, if anyone steps down from the position of President of the Executive Yuan, the ministers would not necessarily have to resign jointly. This is said to be favored by some people. As for this revision of the government organization, it must wait until the Third Plenary Session to be decided. Those who are trying to persuade Wang to stay again pleaded with Wang yesterday to temporarily maintain the affairs of the Executive Yuan until the Third Plenary Session is convened and he resigns, and said that since Zhang Xueliang has already been dismissed, the proposition has already been fulfilled, so there is no need to be stubborn again, causing the political hub to be interrupted. It is heard that Wang said that the wording of his previous telegrams must be taken into account, and he is not deliberately trying to get rid of politics. If it can be within the limits of not violating his previous words, he should be able to accommodate the great kindness of all parties to retain him. As for the matter of resuming the position of President of the Executive Yuan, those who are trying to persuade him to stay are planning to issue a statement that takes into account his previous words, so that the people of the country will know that Wang's temporary expression of resignation was actually to implement the proposal to dismiss Zhang, and there are no other hidden intentions.

▲ Cai Yuanpei's Speech A reporter from the New Sound News Agency visited Cai Yuanpei, President of the Academia Sinica, yesterday and conducted the following interview: (Question) After Mr. Wang firmly resigned as President of the Executive Yuan, he strongly recommended you to take the position. It is also heard that Mr. Wang met with you once yesterday morning (the 15th). I wonder what your intentions are? (Answer) I always hope that Mr. Wang can resume his position. I really cannot take the position. (Question) At this time of national crisis, and you are also highly regarded by the public, it seems that you cannot be too modest. (Answer) In times of national crisis, we should work together, but we should also work hard to the best of our abilities. My inability to serve as President of the Executive Yuan is the same as my inability to fight against Japan like Ma Zhanshan and Cai Tingkai. (Question) If Mr. Wang is determined not to return to the position of President of the Executive Yuan, in your opinion, who would be the most suitable person? (Answer) I think Vice President Song is the most suitable, because the position of Vice President of the Executive Yuan is established by law, precisely to perform duties on behalf of the President of the Executive Yuan when he is absent. And if he is promoted directly this time, he will be familiar with the work. In addition, Minister of the Interior Huang Shaoxiong is also a very suitable person. (Question) Mr. Tang Youren visited Mr. Cai today. Can we hear about it? (Answer) It was not for Mr. Wang's matter. It was to discuss the issue of Zhongda (Central University), because the issue of the collective resignation of Central University needs to be resolved in tomorrow's Central Political Conference. (Question) When will you return to Beijing? (Answer) I still need to continue discussing the Zhongda issue with Mr. Yang Xingfo, so I will not go to Beijing for the time being.

▲ Gu Mengyu's Remarks Minister of Railways Gu Mengyu took the night train to Beijing last night at 11:00 PM. A reporter from this newspaper interviewed Gu on the train last night. According to him, Mr. Wang originally planned to go to Beijing together tonight (i.e., last night), but due to some matters, he will depart tomorrow (i.e., today) to attend the Central Political Conference and report the reasons for his resignation. Then, he will go to Lushan in the middle of this week to meet with Chairman Lin and Military Affairs Committee Chairman Jiang to discuss future national plans. However, Wang has expressed a firm attitude not to resume the position of President of the Executive Yuan. As for the successor, it is estimated that it will be decided after the meeting between Lin, Jiang, and Wang in Lushan.

▲ Wang and Song Fly to Beijing According to reliable sources, Wang Jingwei has decided to take a Sikorsky plane to Beijing with Song Ziwen at 6:00 AM this morning to attend this morning's Central Political Conference. The Sikorsky plane has been repaired and is parked at the Hongqiao Airport waiting for orders. In addition, Song's personal luggage and servants have already taken the night train to Beijing last night.

Japanese Troops Cross the Border to Demonstrate, City Government Protests to the Japanese Consul Yesterday

Regarding the incident a few days ago where dozens of Japanese Marines drove more than ten armored vehicles to the Jiangwan Sports Association Road area to demonstrate, the Municipal Public Security Bureau has investigated and reported the details to the City Government. Problems with the Draft Agreement on Building Roads Beyond the Border

▲ The Bureau of Public Works Has Full Power to Negotiate

▲ Not Subject to Interference from the Consular Body

According to the Dalu News, regarding the draft agreement on building roads beyond the border, a reporter from the Dalu News learned three important pieces of news yesterday (the 15th) from responsible sources: (1) The Consular Body has replied to the Bureau of Public Works that it has received the draft agreement and has distributed it to the consuls. It is heard that the reply from the Consular Body did not include any opinions. (2) It is claimed that the Consular Body believes that the acceptance of the draft agreement should be decided by the Bureau of Public Works because the agreement does not conflict with the Yangjingbang Regulations or change the status of the International Settlement. (3) Sending the draft agreement to the Consular Body is only for notification and not to ask the Consular Body to take any action. Yesterday, the reporter from the Dalu News visited various consuls, but they all refused to discuss the matter or disclose the content of the draft agreement, only stating that they had received the draft agreement. According to the current situation, some consuls in the Consular Body are not in Shanghai. Therefore, if the Consular Body wants to jointly discuss the agreement, it will likely have to wait until next month. However, based on the news obtained by the reporter from the Dalu News yesterday, it can be interpreted that, with regard to the International Settlement, the Bureau of Public Works has full power to negotiate with the Shanghai local officials on building roads beyond the border and is not subject to interference from the Consular Body, as long as the Yangjingbang Regulations are not modified. Moreover, according to the person who revealed this news yesterday, when the Bureau of Public Works and the Shanghai Municipal Government agreed on the garbage issue a few days ago, it was not necessary to consult with the Consular Body or seek its approval. The issue of building roads beyond the border is the same in principle, so it does not seem necessary to consult with the Consular Body or request its approval. If the Shanghai Municipal Government and the Bureau of Public Works are consulting and resolving an important issue for the benefit of the public, why should the Consular Body interfere? Based on this, and considering the recent actions of the Shanghai Municipal Government and the Bureau of Public Works, and the fact that the Consular Body does not seem likely to interfere, the date of its establishment and implementation should not be far off.

Japanese Goods Still Pour into Shanghai

▲ Yangtze River Japanese Ships Do Not Charge Third-Class Fares

Japanese goods continue to pour into Shanghai unabated these days. Yesterday, the Japanese ship Kasado Maru arrived in Shanghai with 13,543 pieces of Japanese goods, mainly textiles, silk fabrics, rubber products, stone powder, medicinal materials, and matchstick raw materials. There were also 1,600 bags of Eastern sugar and more than 400 pieces of gauze, which were transferred to Hankou. These inferior goods were all unloaded in Shanghai. The Japanese ship Ikoma Maru also arrived with more than 10,000 pieces of inferior goods, which were also unloaded at the Mitsubishi and Huishan wharves.

It has been more than half a year since Chinese people have taken Japanese ships on the Yangtze River. In order to revive business, the Japanese are advocating free rides. This time, a certain Japanese ship went downstream from Hankou and has implemented a policy of not charging third-class passengers for fares in Hankou, Jiujiang, and other places. Therefore, the first group of third-class passengers who took a free ride on a Japanese ship to the east numbered more than 600.

Commissioner Jin Arrives in Songhu to Take Office

After the Ministry of Military Affairs dispatched Jin Zhishang, an official of the ministry, to take over as the commissioner in charge of the Wusong Fortress Battery, Jin had previously come to Shanghai to negotiate the takeover and personally inspected the Wusong and Shizilin Second Batteries. He then returned to Beijing to report everything. It is now learned that Jin arrived in Shanghai on the night train the day before yesterday and immediately went to Songhu to take up his position as commissioner. He is currently actively organizing.

Dai Ji Has Resumed Normal Office

Dai Ji, commander of the Songhu Garrison Command, had repeatedly requested the Central Military Commission to resign due to illness, but he was earnestly persuaded to stay. Commander Dai went to Wuhan at the end of last month to meet with Chairman Chiang and personally tendered his resignation. He was again earnestly persuaded to stay by Chiang. Commander Dai, moved by Chiang's sincere words, agreed to withdraw his resignation and has been working at the Garrison Command as usual since the day before yesterday.

Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs Sends a Large Number of Police to Shanghai

▲ Adding Ordinary, Special High, and Mobile Teams of Foreign Affairs Police

After the end of the war and the withdrawal of Japanese troops, in addition to increasing the Marine Corps to 2,800 in Shanghai, the Japanese also used the excuse that Shanghai is an international commercial center to increase the strength of protecting Japanese residents, transferred a large number of water police officers from Japan to Shanghai, expanded their police organization, and added various titles such as special high police teams, ordinary police teams, and mobile police teams. They are already in the process of organizing. The details are being investigated and recorded as follows:

▲ Expanding the Ordinary Police Team The Shanghai Japanese Consulate has an existing team of Japanese police, which is now considered weak. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has specially transferred about 40 water police officers from Japan to Shanghai to be incorporated into the ordinary police team to expand its strength. This ordinary police force is under the jurisdiction of the police department of the Japanese Consulate. The Japanese government's Ministry of Foreign Affairs has specially transferred Mizo Misa, police chief of Mie Prefecture, to Shanghai as the head of the police department to command the ordinary police. He has been notified to come to Shanghai to take office immediately.

▲ Adding the Special High Police Team The Japanese claim that Shanghai is the birthplace of various ideologies and that unfortunate incidents occur from time to time. Therefore, it is necessary to establish a special high police team to specialize in preventing and investigating the intrusion of various international incidents. This special high police team has a quota of 40 people, and it can be increased if the work is busy. In the past three months, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has transferred 60 to 70 water police officers from Moji, Nagoya, Kobe, and other places to Shanghai to serve as special high police officers. They have all arrived. The special high police are also attached to the Japanese Consulate and managed by a police inspector section established by the Consulate. The special high police will submit the obtained affairs to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for review every week.

▲ Adding the Mobile Police Team In addition to the special high and ordinary police teams, a mobile police force has also been added. This mobile police force has a larger scope. Whenever there are matters to be dispatched from Shanghai to various places along the Yangtze River, they can go to serve and are not limited to one place, but can be assigned at any time. Therefore, it is named the Mobile Police Team. Yesterday, the Japanese government dispatched police officers Yoshiga Yukio, Suenaga Junko, Kimori Heiichi, Motoyama Kazutsugu, Ohara Fumitake, etc. from Japan to Shanghai to report to the Japanese Consulate and start organizing this mobile police team.

▲ Dispatching More Foreign Affairs Police The Japanese government also regards Hankou, in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River, as an important area. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has also specially dispatched police officers Oichishi Ichiro and Kawashima Eizo from Japan to Shanghai and transferred them to the Japanese Consulate in Hankou to serve as foreign affairs police. They will leave Shanghai today and go west to Hankou.

Northeast National Salvation Army Sends Telegram Requesting Assistance

▲ Telegram to the Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association

The Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association received a telegram yesterday from Zhou Han, commander of the 5th Route of the Northeast National Salvation Army: (Greetings omitted) "Since our department was inspected, with thousands of troops, the daily food and supplies are not cheap. Previously, the leaders were responsible for borrowing and the local government was making transfers, but this is not a long-term solution. We are grateful that your office promised to be fully responsible for the inspection and sufficient support after the inspection, but we have not received a single penny to date, which has put my younger brother in a very difficult situation. If this continues to be delayed, it will be in danger. Currently, the Japanese bandits are specializing in searching for the leaders of the volunteer army and offering rewards of 30,000 to 50,000, which is deeply lamentable that a few traitors are being used by them. The generals at the front are in danger every day. If we do not provide assistance soon, they may be wiped out. If we continue to rely on the volunteer army to resist and contain the enemy in the interior, it will be too late to regret. In this case, not only will it be difficult to recover the lost territory in the Northeast, but the future of the country is also unimaginable. The situation is becoming increasingly tense. What should we do? We hope to receive a reply soon. With special respect, Commander Zhou Han of the 5th Route of the Northeast National Salvation Army."

Measures for Reducing or Exempting Housing Taxes in War Zones

▲ Proclamation on Reducing Taxes in the Autumn Tax Collection

Cai Zengji, Director of the Shanghai Municipal Finance Bureau, issued a proclamation yesterday, stating: "For the purpose of proclamation, it has been investigated and found that, according to the order of the Municipal Government, the housing tax for one month in the Southern Shanghai District and the area north of the Suzhou Creek in the Pujiang-Songjiang District has been reduced or exempted. A proclamation has been issued to reduce the tax in this year's autumn housing tax in the relevant districts. Now, the original tax bills have been reprinted in red, with the words 'Order to reduce or exempt the housing tax for one month and reduce it in the autumn tax collection. Therefore, in this quarter's housing tax, two-thirds of the original tax amount will be collected.' Also, under the amount of autumn housing tax payable, fill in two-thirds of the actual amount collected (for example, if the original tax is 3 yuan, fill in 2 yuan) to make it easy to understand and avoid malpractices. In addition to submitting a report for record and ordering the relevant tax collection offices to comply and implement, this proclamation is issued for general knowledge."

Housing Rent Arbitration Committee Studies Standards for Handling Disputes

▲ Based on Previous Housing Lease Rules

▲ First, Invite Committee Members to Participate and Provide Opinions

The Shanghai Housing Rent Arbitration Committee has recently faced many housing rent disputes and lacks handling standards, which has caused difficulties. Therefore, it is proposed to formulate lease rules to serve as a guideline. It has recently been heard that, after deliberation by the committee, important articles from the Shanghai Municipal Government's Housing Lease Rules have been extracted and committee members will be invited to participate and discuss them. The committee notified all members yesterday, requesting that they submit their opinions to the committee by the 25th of this month to facilitate discussion.

Establishment of the Exchange Bureau of the Central Bank

The Central Bank established the Exchange Bureau, and held an inauguration ceremony at 8:30 yesterday morning. Directors Ye Zhuotang, Qian Xinzhi, Wang Baolun, Zhou Zongliang, Tang Shoumin, and Chen Xing, supervisors He De, Qin Runqing, and Lin Kanghou, and all employees and many guests attended. President Song Ziwen was unable to attend due to other matters, and Vice President Chen Xing delivered a speech on his behalf, stating: "Today, the establishment of the Exchange Bureau of this bank is a memorable event in the development history of this bank. Back in the spring of the 19th year of the Republic [1930], the government ordered the collection of tariff gold, and in order to meet the needs, this bank specially added a tariff gold exchange section to the business bureau to specialize in this matter. Manager Xi, who was then Deputy Director of the Issuance Bureau, knew that he had rich experience in foreign exchange business. Therefore, he was transferred to Deputy Manager of the Business Bureau to preside over the tariff gold exchange matters. In the past two years, the achievements have been remarkable, and the affairs of the section have become increasingly complex, to the point where it has recently become necessary to establish a bureau. Therefore, it was specially proposed and approved by the Executive Yuan to establish the Exchange Bureau, which, together with the Business and Issuance Bureaus, will be the three bureaus, and Mr. Xi will still be the General Manager. I am deeply convinced that Mr. Xi will be able to handle the work with ease and competence, and I hope that he will still adhere to the principles of this bank and work hard to move forward. This bank will have a brighter future. As for the establishment of the Exchange Bureau, although the organization has been slightly expanded, the various bureaus and offices should still cooperate and work together in harmony. The colleagues of the Exchange Bureau should especially listen to the command of General Manager Xi and work harder. There are high hopes for them." Then, Xi Demao, General Manager of the Exchange Bureau, delivered a reply. The ceremony concluded at 9:00 AM.

The Impact of Price Conversion on Citizens' Lives After the Abolition of Tael and Introduction of Yuan

▲ If the Conversion Ratio Is Stipulated at a Low Rate

▲ Then Citizens Will Suffer Permanent and Immense Losses

The matter of abolishing the tael and introducing the yuan seems to have been suspended recently due to the political situation, but in fact, all preparations have been completed and can be announced and implemented as soon as the central government makes a decision. The Committee for Researching the Abolition of Tael and Introduction of Yuan, organized by the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, has held two meetings to collect opinions from various industries and regions. It is now scheduled to convene a third meeting on the 22nd to decide on a draft plan with concrete measures on the fineness, weight, exchange rate of taels to yuan, and subsequent financial arrangements. In addition, Zhu Yucang, a citizen, sent letters to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, the Chinese Ratepayers' Association, and other organizations, expressing his views on the impact of the price conversion problem on citizens' lives. The details are recorded as follows:

▲ Summary of Opinions from Various Industries The Committee for Researching the Abolition of Tael and Introduction of Yuan of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, in accordance with the resolution of the second meeting of the Committee for Researching the Abolition of Tael and Introduction of Yuan, summarized the opinions submitted by various parties up to August 10, as follows: (1) Regarding the first point, in addition to advocating the Republican Third System, most of them pay attention to meeting the current needs and ensuring that the weight and fineness of the new currency are not too high or too low, or abnormally light or heavy. Old and mixed-color silver coins should be gradually withdrawn, and open inspection and supervision are essential procedures. (2) Regarding the second point, most believe that the circumstances of silver dollar contracts vary from place to place and should be decided by legal groups, together with various industries and creditors and debtors, through public discussion to determine a compromise solution. (3) Regarding the third point, most believe that the issuance of soft currency must have unified measures, and the preparation of cash must be at least 60%, and other debts must not be used as collateral. Moreover, it must be publicly inspected at any time.

▲ Price Conversion Affects Life Citizen Zhu Yucang sent a letter to various organizations, stating: "Greetings. The second of the three issues to be discussed by the Committee for Abolishing Tael and Introducing Yuan is the conversion ratio between silver taels and silver dollars. This issue is directly related to the lives of the three million citizens of Shanghai, namely the following items: (1) Electricity fees; (2) Telephone fees; (3) Land rent; (4) Water fees; (5) Rent, etc. Most of these are paid in silver taels, so they are related to the tael-yuan conversion ratio at the time of the abolition of taels. The difference between the highest and lowest exchange rates of silver dollars this year is 7 jiao and 3 fen and 6 jiao and 8 fen and 8 li, respectively (note that it recently fell within 7 fen). The difference per yuan is more than 4 fen and 2 li. If calculated according to the high rate, each tael of silver is only worth 1 yuan, 3 jiao, 6 fen, and 9 li in silver dollars. According to the low rate, each tael of silver is worth 1 yuan, 4 jiao, 5 fen, and 2 li and 6 hao in silver dollars. Therefore, the difference per tael of Quyuan is 8 fen, 3 li, and 6 hao in silver dollars. For ten taels, the difference is 8 jiao, 3 fen, and 6 li in silver dollars. Electricity, telephone, rent, and other fees are continuous and are not like the debts of loans, which can be terminated after one settlement. Moreover, most of the charging agencies in Shanghai are in the hands of foreigners, and most of the payers are Chinese. If the tael-yuan conversion ratio is stipulated at a low rate, citizens will suffer

Page 14

permanent and immense losses, and it will be tantamount to helping foreigners exploit the Chinese people. Instead of arguing after the fact, it is better to plan ahead. Some may ask, what is a fair tael-yuan conversion ratio? I believe that the current number of silver dollars is only a temporary and abnormal phenomenon and cannot be relied upon. The standard for evaluating the tael-yuan conversion ratio should be the silver content and minting costs of each yuan. After all, no one can deny that the silver content of each yuan has a different value from silver taels, and the minting cost is the cost of processing, which should not be removed. Therefore, the following formulas are obtained: (1) Pure silver plus minting cost per yuan equals the amount of silver per yuan; (2) The amount of silver per yuan divided by one tael of silver equals the number of yuan per tael. (The silver content of our country's silver coins varies, so the most widely circulated one should be used.) My humble opinion is that the right-listed ratio is the fair conversion ratio between silver taels and silver dollars. I dare to offer my humble views for your consideration, hoping that your association will consider and adopt them so that citizens can avoid increased burdens in this era of severe economic oppression and reduce disputes. I would be most fortunate."

Wang Yansong Assumes Directorship of Commodity Exhibition Hall

▲Mr. Wang's Speech Emphasized Production Improvement

▲As Well as Three Points: Leading by Example and Investing in Factory Establishment

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce Commodity Exhibition Hall has always been dedicated to promoting domestic goods and developing industries. Since its establishment, it has been eleven years. Recently, it expanded its premises and added a domestic goods market, making its operations even more proactive. After the passing of its director, Mr. Ye Huijun, due to illness, the Chamber specially appointed Executive Committee member Mr. Wang Yansong to succeed him. Mr. Wang has consistently spared no effort in advocating for domestic goods and serving society with great enthusiasm. He currently serves as the Chairman and General Manager of the Shanghai Silk Industry Bank and is the founder and manager of the Daxin Silk and Satin Store. Yesterday (August 15th) was Mr. Wang's first day in office. He convened a joint meeting of the hall's staff and the responsible parties of the various manufacturers in the hall's domestic goods market. Over ninety people attended, and they had a lengthy discussion. The following is an excerpt of Mr. Wang's speech: Since I have served as a member of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, I have made no significant contributions to various tasks and feel extremely ashamed. Moreover, I find both social work and private business very busy. Now that the gentlemen of the Chamber of Commerce have appointed me to concurrently serve as the director of the Exhibition Hall, I feel somewhat inadequate in terms of energy. However, the gentlemen of the Chamber of Commerce emphasized the greater good and did not accept my repeated refusals, so I reluctantly accepted the position. Our Chamber of Commerce Commodity Exhibition Hall has been established for eleven years. It is open to the public every day for viewing. Its purpose is to promote domestic goods and prevent financial outflows, carrying a significant mission. However, the promotion of domestic goods has become a warning slogan for over a decade. Our compatriots at least retain some impression in their minds, but the result is still that foreign goods flood the market while domestic goods lag behind. The reason for this is not that our people lack patriotism but that foreign goods are cheap and of high quality, which deeply appeals to the mentality of our people, especially women. Furthermore, the reputation of our country's goods has been lost for a long time, and their actual quality is often inferior to foreign goods, leading to a sharp decline. This can be described as the first matter of great distress. From now on, the manufacturer representatives should strive to improve the manufacturing of goods, the sourcing of raw materials, the selection of quality, the study of decoration, the setting of prices, and the convenience of use. They should quickly seek progress to reverse this decline. They must have a firm and unwavering determination to fight to the end before they can achieve success. Recently, I went to Qingdao with the gentlemen of the Chamber of Commerce to investigate commerce. I noticed that Qingdao's efforts to promote domestic goods are far inferior to Shanghai. A manager of a certain cigarette company wears Western suits and consumes imported goods, which can be understood. What is most regrettable is that when he smokes cigarettes, instead of taking from his own factory's products, he buys and smokes foreign cigarettes. This is extremely hateful and shows that the decline of national character has reached its peak. In my opinion, there are only three points to seek the development of domestic goods: (1) Improve production. Our country's domestic goods have always been very rudimentary because there is no long-term research. They only care about immediate small profits, lack a broad vision, and lack a spirit of sacrifice. How can they develop? Those who want domestic goods to develop must first improve their production and be sure to adhere to the principle of truthfulness. They must not have the drawbacks of passing off inferior goods as superior or charging high prices, which hinder the future of domestic goods. This is my first hope. (2) Urge government personnel to lead by example. Since the communists have been rampant, the common people are not at peace, leading to industrial failures and economic bankruptcies. I hope our government will quickly suppress the communists so that industry and commerce can be revived. In the past, the central government stipulated seven local autonomy movements, one of which was the promotion of domestic goods. However, whether government personnel are actually implementing the promotion of domestic goods is something that all our people should pay attention to. They should carefully examine whether what they use is domestic goods, strictly urge them, and even attack them if they do not. Government personnel should lead by example and promote domestic goods to be effective. The best thing is for the government to set up a "Domestic Goods Encouragement Association" to gather broad benefits. This is my second hope. (3) Hope that entrepreneurs will invest in establishing factories. Very few of our country's domestic goods are well-known. Even the silk and tea industries, which have always been famous, as well as one or two recent inventions, are mostly limited by economics and unable to purchase machinery to develop using scientific methods. This leads to domestic goods being permanently in decline. If entrepreneurs can invest heavily in establishing factories, not only will the problem of people's livelihood be solved, but the goods produced will also be very exquisite. Not only will our 400 million compatriots abandon foreign goods and happily use domestic goods, but by extension, it can be popularized worldwide. This is my third hope. In summary, if these three points can be implemented earnestly, it will not be difficult to revitalize domestic goods. I hope that the representatives of this market and the staff of the Exhibition Hall will work together to cooperate and live up to the intention of this Chamber to promote domestic goods, and so on.

The 26th Branch of the Municipal Federation of Citizens' Associations wrote to the General Association of the Municipal Federation of Citizens' Associations and other commercial organizations, stating (excerpt): Unexpectedly, some profit-seeking merchants disregard the nation's pain and transport inferior goods for sale. Japanese Paper Imports Again Occupy the First Place

▲Paper Industry Association Orders Strict Inspection

Among our country's paper products, Japanese imports have always been the most numerous. This is because there are no large-scale paper mills in the country, and the prices of Swedish, American, German, and British goods are too high. Only Japanese goods have convenient transportation and low prices, so they have been able to dominate and occupy the first place. According to an informal report by the Paper Industry Association last year, Japanese goods accounted for more than eight out of ten parts, which is quite alarming. After the Wanbaoshan Incident occurred, followed by the September 18th Incident and then the January 28th Incident, the Japanese paper industry plummeted. Unexpectedly, recently, Japanese goods have suddenly become extremely active again, not only restoring their original sales but also exceeding their previous position. An investigation by the Paper Industry Association revealed that the paper materials imported last month were entirely Japanese goods, with no room for foreign merchants to intervene. The Paper Industry Association is now seeking remedial measures and has issued an order for inspection teams to intensify their inspections.

International Trade Association Pays Attention to the Export of Chinese Goods

▲Goods Must Be Labeled "Made in China"

▲Instructions Must Be Clear and Accurate

The China International Trade Association, in view of the fact that some factories in our country that export goods to foreign countries have not marked the factory name, address, and the words "Made in China" on the packaging and boxes, making them vulnerable to difficulties with foreign customs, and that the product instructions may lack fluency or the wording may be obscure, which hinders sales, specially sent letters to the Joint Association of Mechanical Domestic Goods Factories and the Joint Association of Domestic Goods Factories in this city yesterday, requesting that the above two matters be brought to the attention of the various manufacturers.

(2) Inspection members can use their voucher to board the Yili Steamboat at the reception desk of the Sanmen Bay Port Company at the Dada Wharf at 4:00 PM on the 18th of this month without paying for the boat and meals. (3) After boarding the boat, check the voucher number and your cabin. (4) Please be on time. The steamboat will depart on schedule and will not wait. (5) Please do not change the assigned cabin numbers arbitrarily to maintain order. (6) Our company has set up a reception desk on the boat for the convenience of inspection. If you have any questions, we will serve you sincerely. (7) When inspection members go ashore and get off the boat, please maintain order to avoid danger. (9) Inspection members should return to the boat for accommodation according to the time schedule to facilitate reception. (6) In the afternoon, inspect the planning and facilities for opening the Sanmen Bay commercial port and various locations for fishing, salt production, agriculture, and reclamation. (7) At 1:00 PM on the 21st, take the original boat to Putuo and stay on the boat again. (8) At 7:00 AM on the 22nd, go ashore to visit the scenic spots of Putuo. (9) At 9:00 AM on the 23rd, arrive at Dinghai to visit the Aquatic Products School. (10) At 4:00 PM, take the original boat back to Shanghai.

Silk Factories Return to Normal

▲Turnaround in European and American Sales

There are a total of 113 single and double cocoon silk factories in this city. Previously, due to the sharp decline in the foreign silk market and the plummeting silk prices, many factories suspended operations. Before the summer vacation, only 32 factories in the city were barely operating. Now, with the turnaround in American sales of white silk and the follow-up actions of Britain and France, silk sales have suddenly become smooth. Silk cocoon merchants holding surplus cocoons and the financial sector receiving dry cocoons as collateral have all rented factories to reel silk to meet market demand. As a result, the number of silk factories operating in Shanghai has suddenly increased by 12, bringing the total to 45. As for the 32 silk factories that had reduced their working hours to half a day in the morning due to the implementation of the summer vacation system, they have now resumed full-day work due to the cool autumn weather. As of Monday, all the silk factories operating in the city have returned to their original state before the summer vacation.

British-Owned Public Bus Labor Strike; Capital's Attitude Strengthens

▲Actively Recruiting New Workers; Old Workers Will Never Be Hired

▲Disturbances Occur on All Routes; Workers' Internal Division

After the strike by the British-owned public bus company in the Public Concession, the company's attitude has become increasingly tough. Disturbances continue to occur on all bus routes. Striking workers are warning new workers, and internal divisions are occurring among the workers. Details are recorded below:

▲Warning New Workers; Factory Director and Traffic Superintendent Datte, in order to vigorously find ways to restore the operation of public buses on all routes, has been posting notices at the company's entrance on Connaught Road since the day before yesterday to recruit new workers. Four qualifications are stipulated, and the applicants are overwhelmingly crowded. More than fifty people were hired the day before yesterday, and more than ten people were hired yesterday. Together with the twenty-five people hired before, they have been personally trained by Assistant Manager Pierre. As soon as the training is completed, they will be assigned to serve on various routes. Striking workers, believing that the recruitment of new workers will affect the future of the strike, warned new workers yesterday not to be deceived by the capitalists and undermine the strike discipline. A striking worker forcibly removed the uniform of a new ticket seller at the company's entrance on Connaught Road.

▲Requesting Protection; The Provisional Strike Committee presented a petition to the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Bureau of Social Affairs the day before yesterday, painfully describing the company's oppression and requesting that personnel be dispatched quickly to mediate. At 9:00 AM yesterday, Shi Xiaoshan, Zhang Bailing, Huang Xingmao, He Zhanquan, and others were sent to the Municipal Party Headquarters to request that the Public Security Bureau protect the office of the Provisional Strike Committee in the Xinkang Hotel on Connaught Road and provide assistance.

▲Workers Split; The Strike Committee officially announced yesterday: "Today, a small number of workers are using the name of the Strike Committee to call on striking workers to register at the Xinkang Hotel." The Strike Committee, upon learning of this news, immediately sent people to explain to the masses, saying, "We can only achieve victory by unifying the organization and strengthening unity." A reporter from the New Voice News Agency learned that the provisional committee at the Xinkang Hotel was actually organized by the six worker representatives appointed by the company who were removed by the Strike Committee's resolution. They are the ones who requested mediation from the party and government agencies.

▲Complete Dismissal; A reporter from the New Voice News Agency visited the company's Deputy Traffic Superintendent Charles yesterday and asked about the methods of dealing with the striking workers and the company's policies. He said that all the ticket sellers had not made any demands to the company in advance and suddenly went on strike. When it happened, he was in Japan. Now, the board of directors has resolved to dismiss them all. Moreover, the chairman ordered that when recruiting new workers, no striking workers should be hired. In fact, there is no possibility of recovery. No matter which organization comes forward to mediate, they will only act according to the chairman's orders. If he were in Shanghai, such an unfortunate event would not have occurred. Currently, there is no room for negotiation with the striking workers.

▲Today's Response; The Strike Committee officially announced yesterday: "Today, the company sent 150 'running dogs' to report to the workers, asking them to stop beating White Russians, intercepting cars, etc. A document states that conditions will be answered tomorrow. They also said that if the conditions are not answered tomorrow (i.e., today), they are willing to be severely punished by the masses." The workers all believe that this is a trick to deceive the workers and undermine the strike. The Strike Committee has also notified all workers to gather at the Wuzhen Road Bridge early tomorrow morning (i.e., this morning) to listen to Xu Fu. If the answer is unsatisfactory, they will deal with it together." However, according to inquiries by the New Voice News Agency yesterday, the company denied the matter.

Labor Dispute at the Electric Power Company Resolved

▲Party and Government Agencies Negotiated the Results Yesterday

▲Company Declares Priority Employment of Old Workers

All the workers of the Shanghai Electric Power Company, because the management did not fulfill its promise to give priority to employing old workers, triggered a major labor dispute. Party and government agencies negotiated with the company yesterday and decided on a solution that the labor union representatives considered satisfactory.

▲Labor and Capital State; Zhu Guilin from the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs and Zhang Sheng from the Municipal Party Headquarters, together with Wang Zao, the representative of the Shanghai Electric Power Company Labor Union, went to the Electric Power Company on Jiangxi Road at 9:30 AM yesterday to negotiate with the second shift, Hallett. The labor side stated that the company had declared that since the Sino-Japanese War, the number of electricity users had decreased, which greatly affected business. It was unavoidable to lay off workers, but old workers would be given priority for employment in the future. Now, a new worker has been hired at the Fielun Road Old Factory, and the Transportation Department has temporarily hired a temporary worker, which goes against the promise to give priority to employing old workers. They demanded that the company be ordered to fulfill its promise to maintain the livelihoods of unemployed workers. The capital side stated, "The company's dismissal of workers was a last resort. Moreover, the business has not turned around, and it is impossible to hire new workers. The company has inquired at the new and old factories and there is no hiring of new workers. The carpenter at the 达间 is a specialist, and among the more than 120 people laid off, all were incompetent, which is an exception."

▲Solutions; Representatives of the Party and Government Agencies then advised the company's second shift, Hallett, and decided on the following solution: (1) The company solemnly declares that when hiring new workers or temporary workers in the future, old workers will be given priority. (2) If the workers' addresses are unknown, the company will notify the Bureau of Social Affairs to forward them. (3) Specialists, such as coppersmiths and drivers, who are incompetent among the laid-off workers, are exceptions. Thus, the representatives of the Shanghai Electric Power Company Labor Union were satisfied with the solutions decided upon by the Party and Government Agencies.

Wang Wei'in Cables Yi Peiji to Urge Swift Transfer of Cultural Relics from the Forbidden City

Director Yi, I respectfully write to you. I have recently read in the local newspapers that you have stated that the cultural relics in the Forbidden City will not be moved but will be stored in a warehouse for protection. I believe this is not a good plan. Therefore, I dare to offer my humble opinion. The violent sun has plotted the invasion of our land most carefully, and its destruction of our national culture is also a predetermined conspiracy. Looking at the Shanghai Incident of January 28th, it wantonly threw bombs and set fires, causing our larger cultural institutions, such as the Commercial Press Library, the Oriental Library, and various public and private universities, to be burned down, and the losses were enormous. Now, they continue to attack and invade. Rehe is in danger, and Tianjin and Beijing are feeling the cold. Given their brutality, we must prepare in advance for avoidance and prevention. Therefore, I would like to urge you to quickly select and move the treasures in the museum to preserve the essence of thousands of years. This is to be prepared for a rainy day, which I believe you will consider. The urgent telegram is pressing, and I am respectfully wishing you good health. Wang Weiyin respectfully bows.

Japanese Naval Forces Stationed in Shanghai Held a Memorial Service Yesterday

▲A Lantern Parade Was Held After 7:00 PM

Sugioka, commander of the Japanese naval landing force stationed in Shanghai, had previously issued an order to all units to hold a memorial service for the naval officers and soldiers who died in the Shanghai War at the Benyuan Temple on Zhabei Road at 1:00 PM yesterday. A lantern parade was also held in the evening. Yesterday afternoon at around 1:00 PM, more than fifty Japanese naval landing force officers from warrant officers down attended the memorial service at the Benyuan Temple. About 200 Japanese people living in Shanghai also attended, and Japanese Consul Murai and others also went to pay their respects. Commander Sugioka also gave an extremely激烈的荒謬之 speech. The area around the Japanese Temple was heavily guarded, and pedestrians passing through the area had to undergo strict inspections. This is because the Japanese side was deeply afraid that anti-Japanese elements would mix in and throw bombs, causing another Hongkou Massacre. The memorial service did not end until 5:00 PM. After 7:00 PM, Japanese residents in Shanghai held a lantern parade.

Joint Meeting of Various Organizations in Hongkou

▲Telegraph the National Government to Punish Traitors; Hand Over Power to the People

▲Write to the Court to Release Patriotic Heroes

The Hongkou district branches of the Civil Union and more than 20 groups, including the Hainin Road business community, convened their 20th joint meeting yesterday. More than 20 people attended, and Zhang Xianfang was elected chairman. The following resolutions were passed: (1) To punish the traitor Hu Lifu, a special case should be created in law and the punishment method should be made public to the people to satisfy the public and serve as a warning. The resolution was passed and telegraphed to the National Government for approval. (2) To assist the patriotic hero Yun Huifang, a letter was sent to the court to release him quickly in order to maintain the patriotic movement. Other cases were briefly mentioned. The letters and telegrams are recorded below:

▲Telegram to the National Government Regarding the Punishment of Traitors; Nanjing National Government, be informed. Japan is invading our territory, and our rivers and mountains are changing color. Although the Japanese army is advancing brutally with violence and warships, they are aided by traitors who are helping them to do evil. Internal spies are running rampant, killing each other, and their consciences are lost. Their viciousness is worse than floods and wild beasts. Even if we eat their flesh and sleep on their skin, it is not enough to appease our anger. The so-called crime is a unique case, and is beyond the scope of national law. As it concerns the state and the same race hastening their own demise, the people should be allowed to govern their own sins. No palace or office should restrain them. The people should organize a public court to punish traitors and impose the death penalty to show the public, punish one to warn others, and serve as an example. It should also be printed in historical records and cast in iron statues, like Qin Hui, to leave a bad name for thousands of years and be permanently remembered. During the recent Shanghai war, Hu Lifu, the leader of the traitors, was captured. He will soon be sent to the capital. Although there is a legal precedent for how to deal with him, it is not satisfying. To satisfy the people, the National Government should order the capture agency to hand him over to the people for their own decision and impose the death penalty as a punishment and a warning to future generations. Eliminating the same kind of scum is a national benefit. We hereby inform you and hope you will investigate it.

▲Letter to the Court Supporting Yun Huifang (titles omitted); The people are saddened by the nation's crisis and want to save the Shenzhou from its demise. National salvation must start with self-help in order to resist foreign aggression. Traitorous merchants seek profit by selling inferior goods and using our country's money to build warships for the enemy to invade our country. If these traitors are not dealt with by the people themselves, what will be the consequences? If patriotic heroes form blood soul groups and other people warn each other, there will be no greater patriotic movement. Yun Huifang's comrades have been working enthusiastically and are admired by the people. Unexpectedly, he was arrested, but it is not beneficial to him. Patriotism comes from a good conscience, and he should not be falsely accused of committing a crime. It is the result of the patriotic blood surging. All nationals should deeply praise and encourage him. If all nationals can imitate Yun's actions, Japan will not dare to invade our country's territory. We hope that you will catch up quickly and give encouragement. We urge the court to exercise its legal authority and quickly acquit Yun and release him to maintain the spirit of patriotism so that patriotic heroes can see the light of day and be inspired to save the country. We rely on this action. We earnestly express our words and await the fair judgment.

Public Security Bureau Strictly Interrogates Hu Lifu

▲The Criminal Hu Cries Bitterly

▲No Date Set for Transfer to the Capital

The Zhabei traitor Hu Lifu was transferred to the Third Section of the Public Security Bureau by the Detective Team the day before yesterday. This morning, the Director of the Interrogation Division, Ding Zhibai, personally interrogated him from 7:00 AM to 9:30 AM. It was decided that he would be transferred to the capital for punishment within one or two days. Details are recorded below:

▲Morning Interrogation; At 7:00 AM, Director Ding ordered the police to bring Hu from the detention center. Out of caution, Director Wen temporarily ordered that no one be allowed to listen in. Secretary Han Bing recorded the interrogation. First, they asked about his age, hometown, and address. Then, they questioned him about his relationship with the Japanese, his collaboration with the enemy, his illegal organization of the Shanghai Local Maintenance Association, his recruitment of fake police, his extortion, his running of gambling dens, and other events. Hu also truthfully stated the facts. His confession was no different from what was reported in the newspapers yesterday and the day before.

▲The Criminal Hu Cried Loudly; When the interrogation was over, Hu also knew that his crime could not be escaped and that national law could not forgive him. He could not help but cry bitterly in court, as if he regretted it. He also requested that a people's court be organized to try him, but Director Ding rejected his request and ordered the police to return Hu to the detention center to await orders from the municipal government. Director Ding then immediately compiled the case files and completed the transfer procedures, awaiting orders from above.

▲Director Wen's Conversation; Public Security Bureau Director Wen visited Mayor Wu yesterday to ask for instructions on the issue of Hu's transfer. According to Director Wen, the traitor Hu may be sent to the capital for strict punishment. However, in his opinion, the traitor Hu's crimes are unforgivable, and the public is even more outraged by him. Although the distance between Beijing and Shanghai is short, he fears that the public will become aware of him en route and an accident will occur. In that case, the traitor may be beaten to death before he can be transferred to the capital.

▲Decision to Transfer to the Capital; At around 10:00 PM last night, this newspaper suddenly received a news item stating, "Hu Lifu was transferred to the capital last night." The reporter was very surprised, feeling that even if the criminal Hu was to be transferred to the capital, the procedures would not be so quick. However, thinking that the case was serious and that a quick transfer was possible, the reporter visited Director Ding of the Judicial Section to verify. According to him, the decision to transfer Hu to the capital was made by Mayor Wu after Director Wen asked for instructions from the municipal government yesterday (August 15th). However, the date of transfer has not yet been determined. At the earliest, it will be in two days (August 18th), and at the latest, it may be a week. There is still a question of whether Hu will be handed over to the Capital Garrison Command or directly to the Ministry of Military Affairs after his transfer to the capital. This point will be decided after Director Wen and Mayor Wu discuss it tomorrow (today). In short, Hu's transfer to the capital has now been decided and there is no problem. However, in recent days, some people have often asked me (Director Ding referring to himself) how I think Hu should be punished. It can be seen that Mayor Wu's decision to transfer him to the capital shows the authorities' attention to this case. Therefore, the result of Hu's case can be imagined.

Arrest of Extortion Ring Leader Known for Extravagant Car Rides

▲ Involved in Kidnapping Yan Weilien, Qian Shanfu, Pu Wenting, etc.

▲ A Handgun and Bank Books Were Seized During the Arrest

▲ Two Accomplices, Zhang Afu and Zhang Jiancheng, Were Subsequently Apprehended

A notorious kidnapping ring leader, Zheng Shifan (also known as Zheng Liantang), a local resident with the nickname "Big Brother," 32 years old, has been arrested. He has committed countless kidnapping cases in Shanghai, commanding a large number of accomplices and possessing substantial wealth. He currently resides in a lavishly decorated Western-style house at No. 9, Lane 601, Route Lafayette in the French Concession, using cars for transportation and displaying an extravagant lifestyle. His neighbors all regarded Zheng as a wealthy merchant or high-ranking official, unaware that he was a major bandit. The case was investigated by Jin Jiulin, a detective inspector from the French Concession Police's special division. It was discovered that Zheng, two years ago, organized a gang to kidnap the wealthy merchant Yan Weilien at the Deyilou Teahouse in the City God Temple, and also kidnapped Qian Shanfu, the owner of Yongfeng Timber Company in Nanshi, at the entrance of Pushi Road in the Concord Neighborhood, and further kidnapped Pu Wenting, a native of Wuxi and manager of the Fuxin No. 5 Flour Mill, whose residence was located at a certain number in Siming Village on Avenue Foch. He extorted huge sums of money as ransom for personal use. Yesterday morning at 9:00 AM, Inspector Jin reported to the Western District Chief, and together with detectives Li Yaolong, Zhang Ziying, and constables Qin Youyu and Liu Dianlong, disguised themselves and drove to make the arrest. Upon reaching the destination, the detectives secured the house's surroundings and front and back doors. Inspector Jin, detectives Li and Zhang, armed with pistols, knocked on the door and entered, rushing upstairs to Zheng's bedroom. Zheng, having heard the mixed footsteps on the stairs, knew something was amiss and was about to resist arrest and attempt to escape, but the detectives had already reached the room. He was unable to react and was captured without resistance. Inside the room, they found a handgun, two bank books—one with a deposit of 2,000 yuan at the Dalu Bank and another with a deposit of 8,000 yuan at the Jin Cheng Bank—all of which were taken to the police station. Zheng confessed to the involvement of his accomplices Zhang Ading, residing at No. 30, the intersection of Route Cardinal Fessard and Route de l'Amiral Bayle, and Zhang Jiancheng, residing at No. 27, Gaofuli, Route Sainte-Marie. The detectives subsequently apprehended the two Zhangs, seizing a handgun from Zhang Afu's residence. They were taken back to the police station for interrogation and recording of their statements, and will be handed over to the court for trial. It is reported that Zheng's gang has committed numerous kidnapping cases in the British, French, and Chinese-controlled areas, and only now has he been arrested. Truly, his sins are countless and his crimes unforgivable.

Korean Inventor Sun Changzhi Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday

▲ Welcomed and Introduced by Mu Ouchu and Others

▲ Various Circles in Shanghai Will Hold a Welcome Reception

Sun Changzhi, a young inventor from the industrial arts field, a native of Hampyeong County, Korea, is 27 years old. He possesses extraordinary inventive talent. At the age of 13, he was able to manufacture engines and handguns based on his research. He was arrested for privately manufacturing prohibited items but was released with the assistance of a Japanese lawyer, greatly enhancing his reputation. He then entered Osaka Aviation School, Hanseong Automotive School, Tokyo Commerce and other technical schools to pursue further studies. Last spring, upon graduation, he was hired as a member of the Tokyo Imperial Invention Association, having invented a total of 72 types of industrial products. The Japanese誉 refer to him as the "Edison of the East." He was invited by prominent Shanghai figures such as Mu Ouchu, Sun Hongyi, Wen Zongyao, Yan Zhifang, Li Cishan, and Yin Zhiling, and arrived in Shanghai yesterday (16th) by ship. He plans to test various industrial art products in Shanghai, which will undoubtedly benefit our country's art and education circles. It is reported that the Shanghai Federation of Associations will hold a welcome reception in due course, and it is hoped that all sectors will provide substantial support.

Plague Rampant in Various Places

Due to the prolonged drought, the epidemic is spreading without end. A younger brother named Xu Xiaodi, from the Xu Jiabang village, about two li from Yuepu Township, Baoshan, suddenly contracted the plague the day before yesterday. Xiaodi, being deeply attached to his brother, and his wife nursed him back to health. However, Xiaodi and his wife were infected. Xiaodi's wife died on the same day, and Xiaodi is currently still in critical condition. Since the death of Xiaodi's wife, those infected in the house have emerged one after another, and the situation is quite rampant. Within three days, a total of six or seven people have died, and more than twenty people have been infected. As a result, the villagers in the house are extremely frightened and feel as if they may die at any moment. Even close neighbors dare not inquire about them. Currently, the villagers in the house all close their doors to sleep before sunset and the sun declines. They still dare not get up and open the door until the next day dawns (according to the villagers, they get up quite early). They have to wait until the sun rises before daring to open their doors. The terrifying phenomenon of the plague can be seen here. It is said that when this epidemic is contracted, there is no vomiting or diarrhea, only abdominal pain like twisting, unable to lie down, hoarse voice, sunken fingers, and an extremely strange stench. No matter how strong the body is, upon smelling it, one immediately faints and falls, losing consciousness. In addition, Chen Heshang, a former patrolman of the 17th squad of the 4th district of the Songhu Water Police (because of his short stature, everyone calls him "Short Monk"), a native of Chongming, over 30 years old, has now been discharged from duty. Yesterday, he arrived in Song from Liuhe to look for friends. He suddenly contracted the plague and was in critical condition. He was immediately carried by someone to the Red Cross Third Plague Hospital attached to the Central Medical College on Taixing Road. Unexpectedly, upon arriving at the hospital's entrance, he was already dead. Because he had no relatives or friends in Songzhen, Zhou Lansheng, the local guarantor, reported it to the authorities and collected the coffin for burial. Since the outbreak of the plague in Songzhen, it has been a month, and more than a hundred people have died one after another. The situation is rampant and has not diminished.

Obituary of Huang Chunbo

Huang Chunbo (Canghai), a prominent Fujianese figure in Shanghai, dedicated over 40 years to social and religious education in southern Fujian. He founded over twenty Christian churches and more than ten coeducational schools, nurturing thousands of talents, and his contributions were remarkable and widely praised. In recent years, due to advanced age and frail health, he retired to Shanghai for recuperation. He recently passed away at his residence in Shanghai at the age of sixty-four. His children, Huang Jiahui, Jiali, Jiamo, Jiade, Jiayin, Zhiqin, Renai, Renci, Renhua, as well as his nephews Zhenxiang, Shitian, and Yubin, held a grand encoffining and memorial service yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM at the Universal Funeral Parlor at 71 Jiaozhou Road. Dr. Wan Duoma, a former colleague of Mr. Huang, presided over the service, recounting Mr. Huang's life and achievements. Subsequently, Reverend Wei Shaozeng of Hongde Church offered a prayer. Musicians Ms. Bian Deguo and Ms. Huang Hongbaozhen provided mournful music. A representative of the Chinese National Anti-Opium Association delivered a eulogy. The ceremony was solemn and dignified. The hall was filled with white banners, and wreaths were piled high. Over two hundred mourners attended, including Wang Jingqi, Li Denghui, Chen Binhe, He Dekui, Zhong Ketuo, Xu Jigong, Qiu Hanping, Ma Canhan, Lin Shouchang, Mrs. Cheng Jingyi, and Mrs. Wu Yaoting. After the service, he was buried at the Shanghai Municipal Council Cemetery on Hongqiao Road, with Dr. Wan Duoma again presiding over the funeral. Friends and relatives dispersed around 6:00 PM.

This is truly a benevolent act.

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the Shandong area, the Yangtze River basin, and the coastal areas of China are cloudy and hot with unstable wind directions and scattered thunderstorms. The weather between Japan and the Ogasawara Islands is adverse. The typhoon in the Pacific Ocean is moving northeast-east. Its center was within 120 miles of the intersection of 34 degrees north latitude and 138 degrees east longitude at 2:00 PM. The wind force is unknown. Another center was within 120 miles of the intersection of 19 degrees north latitude and 129 degrees east longitude at 2:00 PM. The wind force is unknown and may have stopped or is moving very slowly. Letter to the Editor

Dear Editor,

According to the manager of the Anle Palace Hotel, upon reading your newspaper on the 11th of this month, which stated that our establishment employs more than 50 Japanese dancers, we were extremely surprised. Since its opening, our establishment has been in operation for more than ten years and caters specifically to Westerners for drinking and dancing. We employ more than 40 Russian dancers, as well as a number of Chinese dancers and Portuguese women, but no Japanese dancers are among them. Fearing that this may cause confusion, we have entrusted our lawyer to write to your newspaper to request a correction in order to clarify the facts. We hope that you will investigate and comply with our request.

Sincerely,

Lawyer Dong Yu

August 16th
