Free Talk

Two or One Branch Talk

Zhang Sheng Cries

— Zhan Lu

Let me introduce a line from the play "The West Chamber," from the chapter "Borrowing the Chamber":

— Zhang Sheng cries, saying: Alas, my parents, you endured hardship to raise me; I wish to repay your profound kindness, but my gratitude is as boundless as the heavens — Miss is a woman, yet she thinks of honoring her roots; I hope the monk will be compassionate, and I will also prepare 5,000 coins to hire a monk to recite scriptures for my parents.

"The West Chamber" has passed, and the modern stage presents "The East Chamber," specifically portraying events in the northeastern region. The protagonist of "The West Chamber" is Zhang Sheng; the protagonist of "The East Chamber" is also Zhang Sheng. Zhang Sheng in "The West Chamber" cries, and Zhang Sheng in "The East Chamber" also cries. Zhang Sheng in "The West Chamber" cries before borrowing the chamber; Zhang Sheng in "The East Chamber" cries after losing the chamber. What is meant by "losing the chamber"? It means that the East Chamber was lost on September 18th. How does Zhang Sheng cry? Zhang Sheng weeps bitterly at a press conference:

— Zhang Sheng cries, saying: I have always acted according to my conscience and have already resigned from the Central Government; this is truly due to compelling circumstances, and I have historical family ties to the Northeast.

Zhang Sheng in "The West Chamber" cries insincerely; Zhang Sheng in "The East Chamber" cries sincerely. The insincere Zhang Sheng opens a new chapter in "The West Chamber" with his crying; the sincere Zhang Sheng ends the old history of "The East Chamber" with his crying.

I wonder which of the two Zhangs is more capable?

I wonder which of the two Zhangs has more initiative?

I won't offer a quick judgment to the questions above; I'll just offer them a couplet:

Peerless romantics as double protagonists,

On the spot, tears shed by two Zhangs.

A Martyr of Jinzhou

— Tian Yu Old Farmer

I recently received a letter from my friend Hu Yuwen from Yuguan, describing the martyr Chen Kaifang of Lianshan. He was arrested in Jinzhou City on the 26th of last month and died unyielding. After his death, the area lost a protector, causing the situation to worsen daily and on the verge of collapse. People inside the pass cried out in grief upon hearing of Chen's death.

Martyr Chen Kaifang was from Lianshan in Liaoning Province. In 1924, he went to Japan at government expense to attend military academy. After graduating, he went to Germany and the United States at his own expense to study industrial management. In the summer of last year, he returned to China after completing his studies. He initially planned to raise funds to develop the rich resources of northern Manchuria. However, before he could unpack, the September 18th Incident occurred, and the public was enraged by Zhang Xueliang's non-resistance and the loss of the three northeastern provinces. He took out his family wealth, recruited soldiers willing to die for the cause, and secretly drilled them in military tactics. Chen was knowledgeable in military affairs and knew that his strength was weak. He often used deception to attack the areas along the false Fengshan Railway. The Japanese army was exhausted from rushing to and fro and suffered significant losses. Therefore, after the Shenyang Incident, the Japanese army did not dare to drive straight into Shanhaiguan, solely because of Chen's disruptive activities in Lianshan. Consequently, the heroes of the green forests in western Liaoning deeply admired Chen's patriotic enthusiasm and were willing to offer their swords to help. Although Chen had only a few hundred soldiers, he could easily call on a hundred in response to an enemy attack. Yuguan relied on this for its safety. The Japanese army, repeatedly defeated in battle, feared him like a tiger. They instructed the puppet state to send envoys to persuade him, offering him 500,000 yen and a large number of weapons and ammunition, and appointing him as the Commander of Western Liaoning. Chen sternly refused, laughing and saying to the envoys, "I am an upright Chinese man and cannot sit idly by as my country falls. However, I am fortunate to be an honest hero. Otherwise, I might as well pretend to accept your offer and, after receiving the military supplies, deal with you later. It would not be too late. You can quickly return and report back to your master and see which country will eventually control these three provinces of Liaoning and Jilin."

The Short History of the Feiying Battleship

— Juemin

The Feiying battleship is sunk. The Feiying battleship was bombed and sunk by the civil war. By chance, I discussed with a friend and got the brief history of it. I will record it in Freedom Talk for those who want to commemorate it.

The Feiying battleship is one of the oldest in the Chinese fleet. It happened to be built at the time of the Wuxu coup. Kang Youwei drove the battleship out to escape. The battleship is the Feiying. Therefore, Kang later wrote a poem about it, with the line "Feiying pursued the waves like mountains." During the Battle of Dharma Protection, Cheng Biguang led the battleship to the south, beginning its belonging to the Guangdong fleet. Afterwards, the boiler was damaged beyond repair, and it was regarded as an abandoned ship for a long time. Bao Luoting came to Guangdong and funded the Kuomintang by using more than 200,000 yuan to buy a new boiler in Germany and give it to the Guangdong government. The Guangdong government also changed the captain of the battleship to a Russian. Bao often held secret party meetings in the battleship. It was once a major base for the communist party's activities. When Li Jishen took over Guangdong, he took this battleship from Hong Kong to the province. He received a warm welcome. The grand occasion was unprecedented. Even today, the people of Guangdong still mention it. Now, unfortunately, due to the conflict between the sea and the land, it was destroyed by a shot from the civil war.

Anyone who knows you knows that your heart is made of iron and it is difficult to change your mind. We left in depression. Later, Chen repeatedly risked his life to infiltrate the Japanese army in disguise to scout out military intelligence. He launched surprise attacks and gained many victories. In the middle of last month, the rebel army besieged Jinzhou. Chen also participated in the siege. However, due to the superior weapons of the Japanese army, they were unable to conquer it after a long siege. Many people were willing to retreat. Chen said angrily: "I am a good Chinese man. If things don't work out, it's God's will. How can I surrender to the Japanese invaders? Kill me quickly." He cursed loudly. He was eventually killed, along with four of his followers. This happened on the 26th of last month. From then on, the Northeast lost a person to rely on, and the situation in Yuguan became increasingly urgent.

As Though on the Water Bank

— Ms. Fujiyoshi

The heat persists. The building residents especially feel sad. It is slightly cooler in the mornings and evenings. My husband often takes a walk. He is accustomed to country living and does not like the hustle and bustle of the city. One day, Ms. Liang Saizhen, introduced me to a swimming pool. I thought that city women only care about dressing up. They sleep late into the morning, enjoying their dreams. Moreover, the harsh sun shines so that the fair skin turns the color of soy sauce. Saizhen argued: "You are talking about rich ladies and flirtatious women. New young people value sports above all else. Swimming is even a specialty in schools. Natural beauty lies in healthy muscles. What's wrong with black and white? Without saying more, watch me try." So, we visited this morning.

Mingyuan was once a place for dog racing. The road is very far. The car travels for about an hour. The morning light is faint. The cool breeze blows. It makes me feel very happy. After buying tickets and entering, we walked to the pool. There is still about a mile away. My weak body is wet from sweating. The pool is two acres in size. The spring water is rippling. From shallow to deep, the water is clear and you can see the bottom. There are only three or five Westerners bathing. Saizhen changed clothes and jumped in, splashing water everywhere. I couldn't see her. In a moment, her beautiful body gradually rose, her pretty face showing shyness, as if she was given a bath in Huaqing. I am afraid that the Taizhen of that year was not as beautiful. I sat under an umbrella, watching her sometimes fast, sometimes slow, going up and down as she wished. Sometimes she used her hands, sometimes her feet, and sometimes she used all four limbs. It was flexible and charming. The Western angel could not hope to catch up with her. I suddenly remembered the women in the villages, who also bathed in the clear streams after working in the fields. When I saw Saizhen's skills, they were extraordinary. I realized that yesterday's speech was not a lie. She also said to me: "My sister, Saizhu, has better skills than me. She can lie on the bottom of the pool and rise after five minutes. If there is a chance in the future, you will witness this." As noon approached, the swimmers gradually gathered. Saizhen enjoyed herself and forgot to go back. My husband couldn't wait any longer and urged her to get up. I heard that many movie stars at sea are good at swimming. Why don't we make an appointment to get together and show our strengths? I know the results will be impressive. Don't say I'm a busybody.

Promoting Domestic Films and Resisting Foreign Films

— By Yi Zhou —

Shouting slogans, posting banners. Once the slogans are shouted and the banners are posted, the matter is considered finished. The biggest problem with modern Chinese people is that they only put effort into their mouths and pens, but are unwilling to use their hands to do things practically.

"Promote domestic films, resist imported films." These two sentences have become the only central slogan in the film industry and the only banner. But unfortunately, this slogan and banner, like ordinary slogans and banners, are just a facade on the lips and in writing, and there is no real action behind them.

Promoting domestic films and resisting imported films are truly causally related. To promote domestic films, we must resist imported films. To resist imported films, we must promote domestic films. But if we were to first ban the import of foreign films and then promote domestic films, that is absolutely impossible. Only by first improving the "quality" of domestic films, so that the minds and eyes of the people gradually turn to domestic films, will we naturally achieve the effect of resisting imported films.

The current film industry, on the one hand, shouts slogans about promoting domestic films, and on the other hand, produces crude and inferior films to deceive the audience and disappoint them. At that time, even if the audience has enthusiasm for supporting domestic films, it will drop below zero. The result is driving fish into the deep and scaring birds into the thickets, driving the audience to foreign film cinemas. Therefore, to promote domestic films, the film industry must do things practically, producing some valuable films. Otherwise, simply following the old path of shouting slogans and posting banners is truly a disgrace to the film industry.

Due to the surging power of foreign sound films in recent years, the Tianyi Film Company has decided to specialize in shooting sound films to resist this trend, as domestic silent films are almost being eliminated. Recently, they have also spent a lot of effort and money to produce a war romance film, "Two Orphans on the Battlefield." It is said that the theme, plot, acting, sets, lighting, sound, etc. of this film are no less than those of foreign films. This may have some effect in resisting foreign films.

I believe that to promote domestic films, on the one hand, we should pay attention to improving "quality," and on the other hand, we must also pay attention to increasing "quantity." Otherwise, supply will not meet demand, and the effect of resistance will be very weak. Therefore, a comprehensive plan to promote domestic films and resist foreign films truly depends on the efforts of the entire Chinese film industry.

▲ To Mr. Hongliu. Please indicate your address. I have something to ask you. Sincerely, the Free Talk Editorial Department

Idle Chat at the Viewing Studio

— Gan Yi

▲ Wu Tingfang

Wu Tingfang was the earliest to study in the United States and the earliest to earn a doctorate. After returning to China, he became a lawyer in Hong Kong. Hong Kong was originally Chinese territory but leased to the United Kingdom, so the registration of lawyers required the permission of British officials. Tingfang knew many foreigners, so he obtained it without much effort. At that time, the Qing court was vigorously discussing diplomacy, which they called foreign affairs. Governor-General Li Hongzhang especially advocated it. He heard of Tingfang's name and recruited him to his office, entrusting him with important responsibilities in foreign affairs. He was repeatedly recommended to the rank of Daotai. Later, he was sent as an envoy to European and American countries. After returning to the court, he was appointed as Vice Minister of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. He did not attach himself to powerful figures and was not promoted for several years. He requested to retire and lived at sea, building a residence called Guandu (Viewing the Ferry), intending to spend his remaining years there. When the Xinhai Revolution broke out, the northern and southern sides resolved the situation through peace talks. Tingfang was elected as the chief representative of the South, firmly advocating democratic republicanism. Tang Shaoyi, the northern representative, was moved by him and sent a telegram to Yuan Shikai, saying that the peace talks would not succeed without it. Finally, Yuan Shikai agreed to his proposal. Sun Yat-sen assumed the provisional presidency in Nanjing, appointing Tingfang as the Minister of Justice. After the unified government was established, a Merit Bureau was established, and Tingfang was awarded the first-class order of merit to commend his achievements. For the next five years, he did not participate in politics but occasionally appeared in telegrams regarding political upheavals. After Yuan Shikai's death, Li Yuanhong succeeded to the presidency and changed the cabinet, appointing Shaoyi as the Minister of Foreign Affairs. Zhang Xun and Ni Sichong, local officials, jointly attacked Shaoyi. Shaoyi resigned in anger. Yuanhong remembered Tingfang's support for the republic and his contributions to the country, so he appointed him to succeed Shaoyi. His son, Zhao Shu, was then serving as a counselor in the ministry. Knowing that his father was about to arrive, he requested to be excused. After Tingfang took office, he said that he had not heard of politics for a long time and was too old to be impatient. He suggested that Zhao Shu be appointed as the deputy minister. The president agreed. Father and son served in the same ministry, which was praised as a beautiful story. Tingfang's actions in not avoiding his relatives were no less than those of the ancients. At that time, Duan Qirui was the Premier. His political views differed from those of Huang Xing. The conflict between the president and the premier intensified. Huang Xing dismissed Qirui, appointing Tingfang as acting prime minister. He soon resigned and went to Guangdong to serve as the president of the military government. He ate vegetarian food for many years, claiming that he would live to be over two hundred years old. However, he died of illness due to shock during the Guangzhou incident. He was unable to enjoy his long life. Was it the will of heaven?

New York Stock Market Rebounds

(Report from American Eastern Banking Corporation)

After a sharp drop last Friday, the New York stock market experienced a chaotic Saturday. However, this Monday, the market rebounded, with prices rising across the board, some by as much as five points. Trading volume, however, was not robust, with only 1.7 million shares traded throughout the day, which was less than the volume traded in half a day on Saturday. The rapid rebound on Monday was mainly due to continued price increases, which stabilized investor sentiment. However, President Hoover's speech remained deeply imprinted in people's minds, so investors were not overly enthusiastic. Based on the current situation, the stock market seems likely to trend upward. The Dow Jones Index is attached for reference:

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Opinion

A Few Words in Response to Three Gentlemen (Continued)

Mr. Rose said, "If you think you have been bullied, it is fundamentally wrong not to study them again." I think that if one is bullied, it is indeed wrong to never study their knowledge again. However, it is also wrong to study their knowledge while being insulted and oppressed by them. As for me saying that anyone with a little heart would not want to go to Zhabei and Hongkou because the traces of Japanese cruelty left behind are unpleasant to see, Mr. Rose said, "We should (perhaps not this 'should') go every day, every hour, to make people see these cruel traces more and get a deep impression." These are different personal feelings and different viewpoints. In fact, my saying that I don't want to go is indeed useless, and Mr. Rose saying to go every hour, every day, or even to live and sleep there, I am afraid it is also in vain.

Person

Mr. Rose also said, "Studying in Japan and other countries should change the previous plan." This issue is Mr. Rose's freedom to express his opinion, and there is no need to criticize it. However, I will take this opportunity to say a few words. I have been insulted and abused by foreigners, and this is not the first time. In particular, I have been bullied by the Japanese even more. Have you ever asked a few students who went abroad to study if they have changed their direction?

Mr. Xingnan said, "According to Mr. Fo, under the active aggression of Japanese imperialism, Chinese students should absolutely not go to Japan to study. However, were not the Opium War, the Anglo-French Allied Forces, the Sino-French War, and the Eight-Nation Alliance also active aggression of imperialism? If so, not only should we not go to Japan, but we should also not go to countries like England and France." That is not wrong, but during the Opium War and when the Eight-Nation Alliance entered Beijing, did Mr. Xingnan ever hear or see any students going to countries like England and France? I am afraid that their studies were either before or after the wars. This point shows the weakness of national patriotism today, which is not as good as before. Even in intellectual circles, there is such a phenomenon, almost as if China's country, China's land, and China's compatriots have absolutely no relationship with me from which country, and it does not matter to me if the country is destroyed, I will go to study anyway.

Mr. Xingnan also said, "In my opinion, academics do not distinguish between territories," etc. In simple terms, it seems that academics have no borders. That does not seem wrong, but I would like to add a condition: If you set aside the concept of the country and personal integrity, but only know that academics have no borders, it is a very dangerous thing. In this era of seeking knowledge, we only know that academics have no borders. In the future, in the era of working, we only know that occupations have no borders and that money has no borders. Therefore, one can be a traitor or a treacherous merchant. If I go further, I am afraid that Mr. Xingnan will have nowhere to stand. I will leave some room and not say everything.

The first mistake in this kind of talk is to only know academics and forget everything else. It is truly worthy of being the tone of a good student. Rare, rare. I will now take a famous traitor as an example. Hu Lifu, the traitor from Zhabei, was recently arrested by the Public Security Bureau. Please Mr. Xingnan take a look at Hu Lifu's confession. The reason he gave is more beautiful than your statement that academics have no borders. He said, "If the local area is not maintained, the people will not be able to sleep peacefully because of the influx of people from Jiangbei." Therefore, the local maintenance association they organized was entirely for the benefit of the local people. Please Mr. Xingnan think about it, for the sake of academics, they forgot the country and forgot integrity. Hu Lifu, for the sake of the local area, also forgot the country and forgot integrity. What Mr. Xingnan said was only for personal learning, but what Hu Lifu said was for local security. Is his topic not more practical and far-reaching than what Mr. Xingnan said? Why does everyone call him a traitor?

Hu Lifu maintained local security under the hostile behavior of the two countries. Several students (referring to several students who studied in Japan after the September 18th Incident, please do not misunderstand) went to give money to the enemy country under the hostile behavior of the two countries to learn their language and writing. Are the mentality of these students worse than Hu Lifu's?

This kind of letter is worthless to respond to, but if I do not make it clear, I am afraid that your confusion will never be solved, and it will cause misunderstandings among former and future students studying in Japan. Therefore, I do not hesitate to say everything to inform you. If you think you can definitely go now, it is your freedom, and I have no right to force you. However, I want to tell you again that not only do I oppose students studying in Japan now, but Japan also does not welcome Chinese people to study there. Please do not go astray.

Originally, I did not want to get into a war of words with others because everyone has their own opinions. I cannot force others to agree, and others cannot force me to agree. Because you want me to respond, I cannot but say a few words. In the future, whether you scold me or laugh at me, I will only laugh it off and not bother with this idle air. Respectfully replied,

Literature

Farewell to My Wife Before Joining the Army

— Ms. Amei

Changing love does not forget saving the country, saving the country is worthy of love. The Northeast has fallen, and the building is about to collapse. It is an opportunity for heroic sons and daughters to serve the country. Therefore, I write two poems of farewell to my wife and send them to patriotic heroic sons and daughters for their review.

The bright moon is still in the sky, the morning rooster has urged me to rise, a man promises his body to the country, generously bidding farewell to his wife and children. Zheren kisses my chest, Zheng Guan kisses my head, parting is imminent, tears fall silently. Wave goodbye from here, go to drink the dragon's blood. My body marches towards the outside of the pass, my soul resides in my chamber. Alas, my soul resides in my chamber, kill the enemy with the same heart.

From the Army to My Wife

The morning wind points to the military flag, the morning sun shines on the military cap, waking up in the morning to touch my head, unknowingly looking at each other and smiling. With the enemy, I have no home, with the enemy, I have no country. A man serves the country, who does not have a heavenly duty? I remember you kissing my heart, I remember you kissing my head, although my body is separated from you, my heart belongs to you. Live to be my hero, die to be a great ghost. Day and night I recite your words, raising and lowering my head I see your face. Alas, raising and lowering my head I see your face, my long whistle is like a rainbow.

Science

Rayon and its Manufacturing Method

— Yao

Silk is originally a natural product, and China has a very large output. It occupies a very important position in exports. However, in recent years, after rayon was invented in Europe, the United States has tried its best to study and improve it. Today, rayon has become an imitation of natural silk, and is the only beautiful raw material in silk fabrics. Therefore, China's silk industry has declined invisibly. From a scientific point of view, the materials and luster of rayon in the future will definitely be better than natural silk. At that time, natural silk may even be eliminated. Therefore, if the Chinese want to maintain their previous authority in the silk industry, they must quickly study rayon and its manufacturing methods.

The raw material of rayon is a carbohydrate fiber. This raw material is an organic substance that grows in plants. For example, the fine filaments of cotton and hemp contain this carbohydrate fiber. The main component of small trees or vegetables is also carbohydrate fiber. It is just that trees are different from other plants in that when they grow up, the fiber and wood can gather together to create the hardness of the trees. Therefore, we can no longer extract them as raw materials for rayon.

There are four methods for manufacturing rayon. However, in industrial manufacturing, the equipment and devices are very complicated, so it is not convenient to describe them in detail in this short article. Now, I will only write down the general steps of these methods and the chemical changes contained therein so that everyone can get some concepts of rayon making methods.

(1) Put cotton in dilute sulfuric acid and dilute nitric acid to turn it into nitric acid fiber. Dissolve this nitric acid fiber in ether and alcohol. Then we get a kind of Colldlon (chemical name, this material can be used to make photos). Place Colldlon in an instrument with fine holes at the bottom, and use air pressure to press this substance out of the small holes like putting on water powder. Therefore, a silk-like thing has appeared. Then add sodium hydrosulfide to this silk-like thing to remove its original nitrate. Then you get rayon. Then pick up this fine silk, hold the two ends, and dry it in hot air, then pack it and send it to the market.

(2) Boil cotton in water. After the bleaching procedure, dissolve it in a solvent of cuprous oxide and hydrogen hydroxide to make a solution. This solution is rayon. As long as you put it in an instrument with small holes in the bottom and squeeze out the thin silk, then bleach, stretch, and dry it, it becomes rayon.

(3) Add sodium hydroxide to the fiber in wood to make soda fiber (Sodacellulose). Then add carbon disulfide and sodium hydroxide to make a solution. Then press it into thin silk. To add sodium sulfide to completely remove the sulfur contained in the silk, and it becomes pure cellulose rayon.

(4) Put the fiber in hydrochloric acid and anhydrous acid to make cellulose acetate. Then add acetone (Acetone) to make a solution. Then apply appropriate pressure to make it into thin silk, and then it becomes rayon.

Social Improvement Discussion Group

Replying to Mr. Zhen's Question on Gender Equality

— Zu'e

After reading Mr. Zhen's question on gender equality, just as he said, "It is still a pending case, not yet resolved." We cannot find the basis of his argument in his article. The few irrelevant "factual" examples are just biased opinions from the male perspective! According to Mr. Zhen, women who haven't read Western textbooks are men's slaves, and women who have read them are men's toys. Regardless of whether Mr. Zhen has other intentions, in terms of the essence of gender equality, he doesn't quite understand this issue!

In fact, the issue of gender equality is not about whether it can be resolved or not, nor can it be definitively said that it will only be resolved at a certain time. According to Mr. Zhen's view, old-fashioned women are slaves, and modern women are toys. Then, to be honest, gender equality will never be realized—if a woman who can write "Dear Brother" and say "Kiss me," "I love you" is a man's toy, then a man who can sing "Sister, I love you" or call out "My little lamb," wouldn't he

Page 20

be a woman's toy? Originally, from a woman's perspective, men chasing after women, wearing upright clothes, combing their hair sleek, and devoutly worshipping at the foot of the qipao, isn't this willingly being women's toys!

In the past, society was indeed too unequal to women. "Men roam, women are hidden" is a clear example of gender inequality! Now, all rights and obligations in society are indistinguishable between men and women. In fact, it can be said that gender equality has already been achieved. As long as we sincerely treat this issue, we can resolve the issue of gender equality anytime, anywhere. Otherwise, under the general concept of still being male-centered and viewing women as "women are always women," even if there are opportunities for gender equality, realization will ultimately not be possible! Just like Mr. Zhen's criticism and observation of women, it will similarly hinder the issue of gender equality!

Gender equality should indeed come from women's self-awareness and self-respect, but men should abandon the concept of "male-centered thinking" and assist women's self-awareness and give women opportunities to resolve it. It is absolutely wrong to simply blame women under certain circumstances and certain abnormal situations!

Written at Leisure

The Life of a Young Mistress

— Shiben

"A Cui! Quickly light the lamp," Wang, the young mistress, lying on the dazzling copper bed, shouted sleepily, just waking up from a dream. While shouting, on her oily, smooth face, which hadn't been powdered yet, she still had a half-awake expression. At the same time, a pair of pretty eyes and a rosy mouth repeatedly yawned, with tears and mucus, showing the emergency and panic in Yanhua Cave (a euphemism for a brothel or a luxurious boudoir).

"Oh! Coming, madam. Why did you wake up so early today? It's only one o'clock," a fifteen or sixteen-year-old maid, hearing her mistress's call, knew that the young mistress wanted to have her "electric charge" (smoke opium). She immediately moved the opium tray, which she had just wiped clean on the beauty couch, to the young mistress's bedside, squatted down, and began to do her only job: packing the opium pipe. For a while, the clear smoke curled up. Squeak, squeak, A Cui packed a pipe, and the young mistress smoked a pipe. After an hour, A Cui's skill was truly great. She had transformed the young mistress, who was lying on the bed like a living dead person, into a vibrant "heroine" (someone high on opium).

After the young mistress's cylinder (body) was fully charged with electricity (opium), she got out of bed and did some seductive work for men: applying powder, rouge, and lipstick. After all the transformation procedures were completed, the old nanny brought a sumptuous feast. Although it was already three o'clock in the afternoon, almost dinner time for others, the young mistress still considered it her first breakfast.

After using this so-called early breakfast, she went back to bed and had dozens of sweet kisses with her closest bloodless killer (opium). She looked at her watch and thought that Mrs. Zhang had invited guests at eight o'clock, and there were still a few hours to wait. She felt extremely bored sitting at home. It would be better to play four rounds of mahjong before going. So, she immediately called A Cui to summon troops and recruit partners.

In less than a few minutes, Mrs. Li, Miss He, XXX, all came in response. The lonely air in the room was suddenly broken. For a while, there was the sound of swallows chattering and orioles singing, extremely lively. After chatting with the ladies for a while, the young mistress threw out the one hundred and thirty-six tiles to carry out hostile actions.

After four rounds of battle, it was getting late. The young mistress hurriedly ran to the room, did some more touch-ups, came out, jumped into a rickshaw, and told A Mao to pull quickly to Zhang's mansion. When she arrived, Mrs. Zhang had been waiting for a long time and said as soon as she saw her, "You're so busy! We've been waiting for you for a long time." She smiled and said, "Because you invited guests, I had to come, so I can only play four rounds of mahjong before leaving today. Tonight, the XX Theater is showing the XX movie, which is extraordinarily good-looking, and I sacrificed myself for you."

It turned out that Mrs. Zhang's invitation to guests was not what it seemed. The purpose was to gather gambling friends. So, after the banquet was over, the ladies, misses, and young mistresses gathered around. Pai Gow, mahjong, until dawn, the gambling game in Zhang's mansion was dispersed.

On a faintly illuminated XX Road with some hazy conditions, a young woman ran out of the gate of Zhang's mansion, jumped into the rickshaw at the door, and a dozing rickshaw puller, like a lost soul, desperately pulled, and ran forward.

Civil Judgment: Dong Desheng v. Que Guocheng Debt Case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 746.80 taels of silver in debt, plus interest at a rate of 1% per month from February 1st of the 21st year of the Republic of China until the date of repayment. The defendant shall bear the litigation costs.

▲Ruling: Gu Yisheng v. Zhang Songqiao et al. Goods Case (Main Text): The plaintiff's claim is dismissed. The plaintiff shall bear the litigation costs.

▲Huang Chencanmei et al. v. Huang Jinzhou Education Expenses and Delivery of One Person Case (Main Text): The plaintiff's claim and the defendant's counterclaim are both rejected. The plaintiff shall bear the litigation costs for the main suit, and the defendant shall bear the litigation costs for the counterclaim.

▲Zhu Shenlian v. Ms. Chen Renting Case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 185 yuan in rent and shall immediately vacate the house. The defendant shall bear the litigation costs. (Above are for August 13th)
